    DataCaptionFields=VIN,Model;
    OnInsert=VAR
               BookNoL@1109400000 : Record 5025439;
               VehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
               VehLedgEntryL@1109400002 : Record 5025405;
               LocationL@1109400003 : Record 14;
               ContactL@1119427000 : Record 5050;
               VehCustL@1109400005 : Record 5025469;
               CurrPriceStickerNoL@1109400004 : Integer;
               PresentRecRefL@1109400009 : RecordRef;
               PreviousRecRefL@1109400008 : RecordRef;
               TypeL@1109400007 : ',Insert,Modify,Rename';
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, '') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               IF VIN = '' THEN
                 AutomPullVIN()
               ELSE
                 SearchVehicleOverAllCompanies('/VEHICLE-INSERT');
               IF NOT CalledFromBatchG THEN
                 ShowMessage();
               // Start PA040200
               DimMgtG.CopyDimension(DATABASE::Item, DATABASE::Vehicle, "Model No.", VIN);
               // Stop PA040200
               // Start PA035597
               // Start PA036002.27153
               DimMgtG.UpdateDefaultDim(DATABASE::Vehicle, VIN, "Department Code", "Make Code", '');
               // Stop PA036002.27153
               // Stop PA035597

               // Start PA032178.1602854
               "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle";
               IF (GETFILTER("Customer No.") <> '') AND (GETFILTER("Customer No.") <> '''''') THEN BEGIN
                 IF GETRANGEMIN("Customer No.") = GETRANGEMAX("Customer No.") THEN
                   VALIDATE("Customer No.", GETRANGEMIN("Customer No."));
               END ELSE
                 IF GETFILTER("Address No.") <> '' THEN BEGIN
                   IF GETRANGEMIN("Address No.") = GETRANGEMAX("Address No.") THEN BEGIN
                     ContactL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.", Type);
                     ContactL.SETRANGE("Address No.", GETRANGEMIN("Address No."));
                     ContactL.SETRANGE(Type, ContactL.Type::Company);
                     IF ContactL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                       "Vehicle Status" := "Vehicle Status"::"Prospect Vehicle";
                       "Contact No." := ContactL."No.";
                       "Address No." := ContactL."Address No.";
                     END;
                   END;
                 END;

               // Start PA036544
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert, ExitPointSetupG.Type::"Inside 1", '');
               // Stop PA036544

               // Start EU.0004569
               IF VehicleCustIsPrivateG THEN
                 MESSAGE(C_INC_PrivateCust,FIELDCAPTION("Customer No."))
               ELSE
                 IF ("Customer No." = '') AND ("Vehicle Status" = "Vehicle Status"::"Customer Vehicle") THEN BEGIN
               // Stop EU.0004569
                 // Stop PA032178.1602854
                   CompanyInfoG.GET;
                 // Start PA033011.5940593
                   VALIDATE("Customer No.",CompanyInfoG."Internal Customer");
                 // Stop PA033011.5940593
                   UserSessionG.RESET;
               // Start EU.0029855
                   LocationL.GET(UserSessionG.GetLocation());
                   IF LocationL."Internal Customer" <> '' THEN
                     VALIDATE("Customer No.", LocationL."Internal Customer");
               // Stop EU.0029855
               // Start EU.0004569
                   IF CustG.GET("Customer No.") THEN
                     "Address No." := CustG."Address No.";
               // Stop EU.0004569
                 END;
               "Old Vehicle Status" := "Old Vehicle Status"::" ";
               // Start PA032178.1602854
               // Stop PA032178.1602854
               // Start PA032500
               IF ("Make Code" = '') OR ("Model No." = '') THEN
                 IF STRLEN(VIN) = 17 THEN
                   IF WorldManufacturerCodeG.GET(COPYSTR(VIN, 1, 3)) THEN BEGIN
                     "Model No." := WorldManufacturerCodeG."Default Model No.";
                     "Make Code" := WorldManufacturerCodeG."Make Code";
                   END;
               // Stop PA032500
               IF "Model No." = '' THEN BEGIN
                 VehicleSetupG.GET;
                 IF VehicleSetupG."Default Model No." > '' THEN BEGIN
                   "Model No." := VehicleSetupG."Default Model No.";
                   DefineVehicle();
                   ItemG.GET("Model No.");
                   "Make Code" := ItemG."Make Code";
                 END;
               END;
               // Start PA032500
               IF "Make Code" > '' THEN
                 VALIDATE("Make Code");
               // Stop PA032500
               "Creation Date" := TODAY;
               // Check for duplication of VIN
               PresentRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
               PreviousRecRefL.GETTABLE(xRec);
               TypeL := TypeL::Insert;
               VINFunctionsG.CheckDuplicates(PreviousRecRefL, PresentRecRefL, Rec."Make Code", TypeL);
               PresentRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
               VehLedgEntryL.RESET;
               VehLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
               VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF VehLedgEntryL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                 "Model No." := VehLedgEntryL."Model No.";
                 "Make Code" := VehLedgEntryL."Make Code";
                 DefineVehicle();
               END;
               IF NOT OptionG.GET(VIN, 10000) THEN BEGIN
                 OptionG.VIN := VIN;
                 OptionG."Line No." := 10000;
                 OptionG.INSERT;
               END;
               OptionG."Model No." := "Model No.";
               OptionG.Description := Model;
               OptionG.Type := OptionG.Type::Vehicle;
               OptionG."Make Code" := "Make Code";
               OptionG."Built-in Date" := WORKDATE;
               OptionG.Quantity := 1;
               OptionG.MODIFY;
               CurrPriceStickerNoL := OptionG.UpdateArchiv(2, FALSE, OptionG.ReturnManual());
               IF CurrPriceStickerNoL <> 0 THEN
                 "Current Price Sticker" := CurrPriceStickerNoL;
               //Appl. Last Posting No.
               BookNoL.RESET;
               BookNoL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
               BookNoL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF BookNoL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                 "Current Branch Book No." := BookNoL."Purch. Branch Book No.";
               // Start PA038450
                 "Current Book No." := BookNoL."No.";
               // Stop PA038450
               END;
               VehLedgEntryL.RESET;
               VehLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry Type", VIN, "Posting Date");
               VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Entry Type", VehLedgEntryL."Entry Type"::Purchase);
               VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(Vehicle, TRUE);
               VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF VehLedgEntryL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                 "Purchase Invoice Date" := VehLedgEntryL."Posting Date";
                 "Purchase Receipt Date" := VehLedgEntryL."Posting Date";
               END;
               VehLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Entry Type", VehLedgEntryL."Entry Type"::Sale);
               IF VehLedgEntryL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                 "Date of Sale" := VehLedgEntryL."Posting Date";
               END;
               IF VehicleL.GET(VIN) THEN
                 VehicleL.DELETE;
               FindVehicleLabTypeG.Vehicle(Rec);
               "Creation Time" := TIME;
               "License No. Compressed" := CompressLicenseNo("License No.");
               // Start PA032636
               "VIN Check Code" := CollectionUnitG.BackString(VIN);
               // Stop PA032636
               // Start EU.0000044
               "License No. Check Code" := CollectionUnitG.BackString("License No.");
               // Stop EU.0000044
               // Start PA034598
               ServCampFuncsG.SearchOneVehicle(Rec, ServHdrG, ServCampVehG, TRUE);
               // Stop PA034598
               // Start PA036268
               ModifyAllowedCheck(TRUE);
               // Stop PA036268
               // Start PA033985.19039
               UpdateBookNoInSalesIncLines();
               // Stop PA033985.19039

               // Start PA037815
               // Start PA040200
               // Stop PA040200
               // Stop PA037815

               // Start PA041187.87690
               VehCustL.RESET;
               VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
               IF VehCustL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
                 IF (VehCustL."Customer No." = "Customer No.") AND (VehCustL."Contact No." = "Contact No.") THEN
                   VehCustL.DELETE;
               END;
               // Stop PA041187.87690

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnInsert, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post, '');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnModify=VAR
               ServHdrL@20395103 : Record 5025624;
               VehServContrL@20395102 : Record 5061005;
               DocWarningL@1119418000 : TEMPORARY Record 5045369;
               ServCampNegVehL@1101314645 : Record 5025699;
               VehCustL@1109400000 : Record 5025469;
               ServContrMgtL@20395101 : Codeunit 5061000;
               PresentRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
               PreviousRecRefL@1109400003 : RecordRef;
               TypeL@1109400002 : ',Insert,Modify,Rename';
               SkipL@4624100 : Boolean;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, '') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               // Start PA041885
               // Stop PA041885
               "Last Date Modified" := TODAY;
               "Last Time Modified" := TIME;
               SearchVehicleOverAllCompanies('/VEHICLE-CHANGE');
               CLEAR(ServHdrG);
               // Start PA034598.I001660
               ServCampNegVehL.DeleteVIN(VIN);
               // Stop PA034598.I001660
               ServCampFuncsG.SearchOneVehicle(Rec, ServHdrG, ServCampVehG, TRUE);
               // Check for duplication of VIN
               PresentRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
               PreviousRecRefL.GETTABLE(xRec);
               TypeL := TypeL::Modify;
               VINFunctionsG.CheckDuplicates(PreviousRecRefL, PresentRecRefL, Rec."Make Code", TypeL);
               PresentRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
               "License No. Compressed" := CompressLicenseNo("License No.");
               // Start PA032636
               "VIN Check Code" := CollectionUnitG.BackString(VIN);
               // Stop PA032636
               // Start EU.0000044
               "License No. Check Code" := CollectionUnitG.BackString("License No.");
               // Stop EU.0000044
               IF xRec."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" THEN
                 SearchOpenServiceOrder(VIN, DocWarningL, FALSE);
               // Start PA036268
               ModifyAllowedCheck(FALSE);
               // Stop PA036268

               // Start PA037815
               // Start PA037815.38403
               // Stop PA037815.38403
               DimMgtG.CopyDimension(DATABASE::Item, DATABASE::Vehicle, "Model No.", VIN);
               // Stop PA037815

               // Start PA041187.87690
               VehCustL.RESET;
               VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
               IF VehCustL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
               // Start EU.0047174
                 OnModifyBeforeRemovePreviousCustEvent(xRec, VehCustL, SkipL);
                 IF NOT SkipL THEN BEGIN
                   IF (VehCustL."Customer No." = "Customer No.") AND (VehCustL."Contact No." = "Contact No.") THEN
                     VehCustL.DELETE;
                 END;
               // Stop EU.0047174
               END;
               // Stop PA041187.87690
               // Start EU.0203951.207925
               IF Mileage <> xRec.Mileage THEN BEGIN
                 ServHdrL.RESET;
                 ServHdrL.CHANGECOMPANY(CURRENTCOMPANY);
                 VehServContrL.CHANGECOMPANY(CURRENTCOMPANY);
                 ServHdrL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type", VIN);
                 ServHdrL.SETFILTER("Document Type", '%1|%2|%3', ServHdrL."Document Type"::Quote, ServHdrL."Document Type"::Order, ServHdrL."Document Type"::Scheduling);
                 ServHdrL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                 IF ServHdrL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
                   VehServContrL.VehicleSet(Rec);
                   REPEAT
                     IF VehServContrL.ValidContrOfServCustFind(ServHdrL.VIN, ServHdrL."Document Type", ServHdrL."No.", ServHdrL."Completion Date") THEN BEGIN
                       PresentRecRefL.GETTABLE(ServHdrL);
                       ServHdrL.Mileage := Mileage;
                       PreviousRecRefL.GETTABLE(ServHdrL);
                       ServContrMgtL.FindingsModify(PreviousRecRefL, PresentRecRefL, VehServContrL."Serv. Contract Cust. No.", '');
                     END;
                   UNTIL ServHdrL.NEXT = 0;
                 END;
               END;
               // Stop EU.0203951.207925

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnModify, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post, '');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

    OnDelete=VAR
               TechDataValueL@1109400001 : Record 5205856;
               TireHotelOrderHeaderL@1055600 : Record 5208845;
               ErrorTextL@1109400000 : Text[260];
               VehicleServiceHistoryFuncL@1101286982 : Codeunit 5205950;
             BEGIN
               // Start PA032225
               IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnDelete, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, '') THEN
                 EXIT;
               // Stop PA032225

               //do not delete, because if the same vehicle is activated:
               ErrorTextL := '';
               PurchOrderLineG.RESET;
               PurchOrderLineG.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
               PurchOrderLineG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF PurchOrderLineG.FINDFIRST THEN
                 ErrorTextL := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC001, PurchOrderLineG.TABLECAPTION);
               SalesOrderLineG.RESET;
               SalesOrderLineG.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
               SalesOrderLineG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF SalesOrderLineG.FINDFIRST THEN
                 ErrorTextL := ErrorTextL + STRSUBSTNO(C_INC001, SalesOrderLineG.TABLECAPTION);
               ServHdrG.RESET;
               ServHdrG.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type", VIN);
               // Start EU.0036781
               ServHdrG.SETFILTER("Document Type", '%1|%2|%3', ServHdrG."Document Type"::Quote, ServHdrG."Document Type"::Order, ServHdrG."Document Type"::Scheduling);
               // Stop EU.0036781
               ServHdrG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
               IF ServHdrG.FINDFIRST THEN
                 ErrorTextL := ErrorTextL + STRSUBSTNO(C_INC001, ServHdrG.TABLECAPTION);
               IF "Vehicle Status" IN [
                  "Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
                  "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle",
                  "Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle"]
               THEN
                 ErrorTextL := ErrorTextL + STRSUBSTNO(C_INC024, "Vehicle Status");

               // Start EU.0051382
               TireHotelOrderHeaderL.RESET;
               TireHotelOrderHeaderL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
               TireHotelOrderHeaderL.SETFILTER("Order Status",'<>%1',TireHotelOrderHeaderL."Order Status"::Archived);
               IF NOT TireHotelOrderHeaderL.ISEMPTY THEN
                 ErrorTextL += STRSUBSTNO(C_INC001, TireHotelOrderHeaderL.TABLECAPTION);
               // Stop EU.0051382

               IF ErrorTextL > '' THEN
                 ERROR(C_INC002 + ErrorTextL);
               DeleteAddtlTables();
               // Start PA034598
               // Stop PA034598
               DeleteVehStocklist();
               // Start PA034066
               VehicleServiceHistoryFuncL.DeleteThirdPartyRecords(VIN);
               // Stop PA034066

               // Start PA035597
               // Start PA036002.27153
               DimMgtG.DeleteDefaultDim(DATABASE::Vehicle, VIN, '');
               // Stop PA036002.27153
               // Stop PA035597

               // Start EU.0020651
               TechDataValueL.DeleteTechnicalData(Rec);
               // Stop EU.0020651

               // Start PA032225
               ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::OnDelete, ExitPointSetupG.Type::Post, '');
               // Stop PA032225
             END;

                                                                  IF "Vehicle Status" IN [
                                                                     "Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
                                                                     "Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle",

                                                                  THEN

                                                                // Stop PA032589

                                                                // Start EU.0047174
                                                                OnBeforePreviousCustomerUpdateEvent(xRec, SkipL);
                                                                IF NOT SkipL THEN BEGIN
                                                                  VehCustL.RESET;
                                                                  VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                  VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                  IF VehCustL.FINDLAST THEN
                                                                    IF VehCustL."Customer No." = "Customer No." THEN
                                                                      VehCustL.DELETE(TRUE);
                                                                  IF NOT VehicleFromOtherCompanyG THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF xRec."Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                                                      InsertL := TRUE;
                                                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    IF Rec."Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                                                      InsertL := TRUE;
                                                                  END;

                                                                  VehCustL.RESET;
                                                                  VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                  VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                  VehCustL.SETRANGE("Contact No.", xRec."Contact No.");
                                                                  IF VehCustL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                                                    IF xRec."Customer No." <> '' THEN
                                                                      IF CustLibL.IsInternalCustomer(xRec."Customer No.") THEN
                                                                        InsertL := FALSE;
                                                                    IF InsertL THEN BEGIN
                                                                      VehCustL.INIT;
                                                                      VehCustL.VALIDATE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                      VehCustL.VALIDATE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                      IF NOT VehicleFromOtherCompanyG THEN BEGIN
                                                                        VehCustL.VALIDATE("Contact No.", xRec."Contact No.");
                                                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                        VehCustL.VALIDATE("Contact No.", Rec."Contact No.");
                                                                      END;
                                                                      VehCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
                                                                    END;
                                                                  END;
                                                                END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0047174
                                                                IF CustG.GET("Customer No.") THEN BEGIN

                                                                  ContL.SETRANGE("Address No.", "Address No.");

                                                                  ContL.SETRANGE(Type, ContL.Type::Company);
                                                                  IF ContL.FINDFIRST THEN
                                                                    "Contact No." := ContL."No."
                                                                  ELSE
                                                                    "Contact No." := '';
                                                                  IF CurrFieldNo = FIELDNO("Customer No.") THEN BEGIN
                                                                    VehCustL.RESET;
                                                                    VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                // Start PA034254.I000897
                                                                    VehCustL.SETFILTER(Type, '%1|%2', VehCustL.Type::Buyer, VehCustL.Type::Owner);
                                                                // Start EU.0047174
                                                                    IF VehCustL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN

                                                                          UNTIL VehCustL.NEXT = 0;
                                                                // Start EU.0053730
                                                                      CALCFIELDS("Old Customer Name");
                                                                // Stop EU.0053730
                                                                    END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0047174
                                                                // Start EU.0071195
                                                                    IF UserSessionUnitG.TireHotelLicensePermissionCheck THEN BEGIN

                                                                          REPEAT

                                                                            TireHotelOrderHeaderL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                                                          UNTIL TireHotelOrderHeaderL.NEXT = 0;
                                                                      END;
                                                                // Stop EU.0071195
                                                                // Stop PA034254.I000897
                                                                  END;
                                                                END ELSE
                                                                  "Address No." := 0;
                                                                // Start PA042167
                                                                IF "Customer No." <> xRec."Customer No." THEN
                                                                  VALIDATE("Date of Re-motorization", 0D);
                                                                // Stop PA042167
                                                                CALCFIELDS(Name);
                                                                // Start PA042646
                                                                VehicleAppointmentL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                VehicleAppointmentL.SETFILTER("Next Appointment Date", '%1..', WORKDATE);
                                                                // Start PA042646.85679
                                                                VehicleAppointmentL.SETFILTER(Status, '<>%1', VehicleAppointmentL.Status::Cancelled);
                                                                // Stop PA042646.85679
                                                                IF VehicleAppointmentL.FINDSET THEN
                                                                  REPEAT

                                                                    VehicleAppointmentL."Customer Name" := Name;
                                                                // Start EU.0191766
                                                                    VehicleAppointmentL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                                                                // Stop EU.0191766
                                                                  UNTIL VehicleAppointmentL.NEXT = 0;
                                                                // Start PA042646.85679

                                                                // Stop PA042646
                                                              END;

    { 5045650;;Contact No.         ;Code20        ;TableRelation=Contact WHERE (Type=CONST(Company));
                                                   OnValidate=VAR
                                                                ContL@1109400000 : Record 5050;
                                                                Cont2L@1109400002 : Record 5050;
                                                                VehCustL@1109400001 : Record 5025469;
                                                                CustLibL@1109400003 : Record 18;
                                                                InsertL@1109400004 : Boolean;
                                                              BEGIN
                                                                IF ContL.GET("Contact No.") THEN BEGIN
                                                                  IF ContL."Customer No." <> '' THEN
                                                                    ERROR(C_INC042, ContL."No.", ContL."Customer No.")
                                                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                                                    "Customer No." := '';
                                                                    "Address No." := ContL."Address No.";
                                                                // Start PA041856
                                                                    VehCustL.RESET;
                                                                    VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                    VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                    IF VehCustL.FINDLAST THEN
                                                                      IF VehCustL."Contact No." = "Contact No." THEN
                                                                        VehCustL.DELETE(TRUE);
                                                                    IF Cont2L.GET(xRec."Contact No.") THEN BEGIN
                                                                // Start PA041187.87690
                                                                      IF NOT VehicleFromOtherCompanyG THEN BEGIN
                                                                // Stop PA041187.87690
                                                                        IF xRec."Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                                                          InsertL := TRUE;
                                                                // Start PA041187.87690
                                                                      END ELSE BEGIN
                                                                        IF Rec."Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                                                          InsertL := TRUE;
                                                                      END;
                                                                // Stop PA041187.87690
                                                                      VehCustL.RESET;
                                                                      VehCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                      VehCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                      VehCustL.SETRANGE("Contact No.", Cont2L."No.");
                                                                      IF VehCustL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
                                                                        IF Cont2L."Customer No." <> '' THEN
                                                                          IF CustLibL.IsInternalCustomer(Cont2L."Customer No.") THEN
                                                                            InsertL := FALSE;
                                                                        IF InsertL THEN BEGIN
                                                                          VehCustL.INIT;
                                                                          VehCustL.VALIDATE(VIN, VIN);
                                                                          VehCustL.VALIDATE(Type, VehCustL.Type::"Previous Customer");
                                                                // Start PA041187.87690
                                                                          IF NOT VehicleFromOtherCompanyG THEN
                                                                // Stop PA041187.87690
                                                                            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Contact No.", Cont2L."No.")
                                                                // Start PA041187.87690
                                                                          ELSE
                                                                            VehCustL.VALIDATE("Contact No.", Rec."Contact No.");
                                                                // Stop PA041187.87690
                                                                          VehCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
                                                                        END;
                                                                      END;
                                                                    END;
                                                                // Stop PA041856
                                                                  END;
                                                                END ELSE
                                                                  "Address No." := 0;
                                                                CALCFIELDS(Name);
                                                                MODIFY;
                                                              END;

                                                   CaptionML=ENU=Contact No. }

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPointCall@5025380(MakeCoddeP@1109400003 : Code[20];TriggerP@1109400002 : Integer;TypeP@1109400001 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1109400000 : Text[50];VAR EPRecRefP@1109400005 : RecordRef) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      EXIT(ExitPointUnitG.RunExitPoint(
        ExitPointSetupG."Object Type"::Table,
        DATABASE::Vehicle,
        MakeCoddeP, TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefP, EPRecRef2G, ExitPointParamG));
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE ExitPoint@5025450(TriggerP@1119452001 : Integer;TypeP@1119432000 : Integer;ExitPointIDP@1119432001 : Text[50]) ReturnR : Boolean;
    VAR
      EPRecRefL@1109400004 : RecordRef;
    BEGIN
      // @ This local function works as ExitPoint wrapper function. It will control the ExitPointCheck function call.
      // @ It passes thru all the handshake parameter values.
      // @ It takes care to provide the processing records as RecordReference to the ExitPointCheck function.
      // @ When possible a Make Code is also identified and passed to the called ExitPointCheck function.

      // Start PA036544
      EPRecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
      EPRecRef2G.GETTABLE(xRec);
      ExitPointParamG."Called CurrFieldNo" := CurrFieldNo;
      ReturnR := ExitPointCall("Make Code", TriggerP, TypeP, ExitPointIDP, EPRecRefL);
      EPRecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
      CLEAR(EPRecRef2G);
      // Stop PA036544
    END;

    PROCEDURE __STOP_EXITPOINT__@1101342643();
    BEGIN
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateMileage@18884300();
    VAR
      SalesLineL@18884300 : Record 37;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0188843.192508
      // Start PA038140
      SalesLineL.RESET;
      SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type", VIN, "Item Type", "No.", "Order No.", "Order Line No.");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", SalesLineL."Document Type"::Order);
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Item Type", SalesLineL."Item Type"::Vehicle);
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Order Type", SalesLineL."Order Type"::"Vehicle Sales & Purchases");
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Quantity Shipped", 0);
      SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Quantity Invoiced", 0);
      IF SalesLineL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesLineL.Mileage := Mileage;
          SalesLineL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL SalesLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA038140
      // Stop EU.0188843.192508
    END;

    PROCEDURE ModifyAllowedCheck@1101342645(CalledFromOnInsertTriggerP@1101342647 : Boolean);
    VAR
      RecRefL@1101342643 : RecordRef;
      ExRecRefL@1101342644 : RecordRef;
      BlockRecordL@1101342646 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ The function will call the Change Log management CU where the Rec is checked according to the change log setup.
      // @ With CalledFromOnInsertTriggerP you can specify if it was called from the table OnModify or OnInsert Trigger.
      // @ When a Must Field problem gets detected, then the Rec will be blocked.
      // Start PA036268
      RecRefL.GETTABLE(Rec);
      // Start EU.0188843.189774
      ExRecRefL.GETTABLE(xRec);
      // Stop EU.0188843.189774
      IF CalledFromOnInsertTriggerP THEN
        BlockRecordL := ChangeLogMgntG.RecordInsertChangeLogCheck(RecRefL, ExRecRefL)
      ELSE
        BlockRecordL := ChangeLogMgntG.RecordModifyChangeLogCheck(RecRefL, ExRecRefL);
      RecRefL.SETTABLE(Rec);
      IF GUIALLOWED THEN
      // Start PA040590
        IF NOT Blocked THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA040590
          IF BlockRecordL THEN BEGIN
            Blocked := TRUE;
            IF NOT CalledFromOnInsertTriggerP THEN
              UserSessionUnitG.ShowMessageBox(STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_RecordWillBeBlocked, TABLECAPTION, VIN, "License No."));
          END;
      // Start PA040590
        END ELSE
          IF BlockRecordL THEN
            UserSessionUnitG.ShowMessageBox(STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_RecordWillBeBlocked, TABLECAPTION, VIN, "License No."));
      // Stop PA040590
      // Stop PA036268
    END;

    PROCEDURE AssistEdit@2(OldVehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400) : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032500
      VehicleG := Rec;
      VehicleSetupG.GET();
      VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Vehicle Nos.");
      IF NoSeriesMgtG.SelectSeries(VehicleSetupG."Vehicle Nos.", OldVehicleP."No. Series", VehicleG."No. Series") THEN BEGIN
        NoSeriesMgtG.SetSeries(VehicleG.VIN);
        Rec := VehicleG;
        EXIT(TRUE);
      END;
      // Stop PA032500
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateGrossProfit@3();
    BEGIN
      "Gross Profit (LCY)" := "Actual Sales Price (LCY)" - "Unit Cost (LCY)";
      "Gross Profit %" := ("Gross Profit (LCY)" * 100) / "Actual Sales Price (LCY)";
    END;

    PROCEDURE DefineVehicle@4();
    VAR
      EventReturnValueL@2169900 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA036544
      IF ExitPoint(ExitPointSetupG.Trigger::"Function", ExitPointSetupG.Type::Pre, 'DefineVehicle') THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop PA036544

      // Start EU.0027964
      OnBeforeDefineVehicleEvent(EventReturnValueL, Rec);
      IF EventReturnValueL THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop EU.0027964

      IF ItemG.GET("Model No.") THEN BEGIN
        Model := '';
        IF ItemG.Description <> '' THEN
          Model := ItemG.Description;
        Type := '';
        IF ItemG."Description 2" <> '' THEN
          Type := ItemG."Description 2";
        IF ItemG.Class <> '' THEN
          Class := ItemG.Class;
        IF ItemG."Base Unit of Measure" <> '' THEN
          "Unit of Measure Code" := ItemG."Base Unit of Measure";
        "Model No." := ItemG."No.";
        IF ItemG."Statistics Group" <> 0 THEN
          "Statistics Group" := ItemG."Statistics Group";
        IF ItemG."Vehicle Type Code" <> '' THEN
          "Vehicle Type Code" := ItemG."Vehicle Type Code";
        IF ItemG."Vehicle Category Code" <> '' THEN
          "Vehicle Category Code" := ItemG."Vehicle Category Code";
        IF ItemG."Market Segment Code" <> '' THEN
          "Market Segment Code" := ItemG."Market Segment Code";
        IF ItemG."Emissions Test Category Code" <> '' THEN
          "Emissions Test Category Code" := ItemG."Emissions Test Category Code";
        IF ItemG."Engine Code" <> '' THEN
          "Engine Code" := ItemG."Engine Code";
        IF ItemG."Model Code" <> '' THEN
          "Model Code" := ItemG."Model Code";
        IF ItemG."Engine Type Code" <> '' THEN
          "Engine Type Code" := ItemG."Engine Type Code";
        IF ItemG."Transmission Type Code" <> '' THEN
          "Transmission Type Code" := ItemG."Transmission Type Code";
        IF ItemG."Cylinder Capacity (ccm)" <> 0 THEN
          "Cylinder Capacity (ccm)" := ItemG."Cylinder Capacity (ccm)";
        IF ItemG."No. of Cylinders" <> 0 THEN
          "No. of Cylinders" := ItemG."No. of Cylinders";
        IF ItemG."Power (kW)" <> 0 THEN
          "Power (kW)" := ItemG."Power (kW)";
        IF ItemG."Power (hp)" <> 0 THEN
          "Power (hp)" := ItemG."Power (hp)";
        IF ItemG.Tires <> '' THEN
          Tires := ItemG.Tires;
        IF ItemG."Empty Weight (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Empty Weight (kg)" := ItemG."Empty Weight (kg)";
        IF ItemG."Total Weight (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Total Weight (kg)" := ItemG."Total Weight (kg)";
        IF ItemG."Roof Load (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Roof Load (kg)" := ItemG."Roof Load (kg)";
        IF ItemG."Trailer Load (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Trailer Load (kg)" := ItemG."Trailer Load (kg)";
        IF ItemG."Trailer Tongue Load (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Trailer Tongue Load (kg)" := ItemG."Trailer Tongue Load (kg)";
        "4WD" := ItemG."4WD";
        IF ItemG."No. of Axles" <> 0 THEN
          "No. of Axles" := ItemG."No. of Axles";
        IF ItemG."Wheelbase (mm)" <> 0 THEN
          "Wheel Distance (mm)" := ItemG."Wheelbase (mm)";
        IF ItemG."Front Axle Load (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Front Axle Load (kg)" := ItemG."Front Axle Load (kg)";
        IF ItemG."Rear Axle Load (kg)" <> 0 THEN
          "Rear Axle Load (kg)" := ItemG."Rear Axle Load (kg)";
        IF ItemG."No. of Doors" <> 0 THEN
          "No. of Doors" := ItemG."No. of Doors";
        IF ItemG."Gen. Prod. Posting Group" <> '' THEN
          "Gen. Prod. Posting Group" := ItemG."Gen. Prod. Posting Group";
        IF ItemG."VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> '' THEN
          "VAT Prod. Posting Group" := ItemG."VAT Prod. Posting Group";
        IF ItemG."Labor Type" <> '' THEN
          "Labor Type" := ItemG."Labor Type";
        IF ItemG."Labor Charging Code" <> '' THEN
          "Labor Charging Code" := ItemG."Labor Charging Code";
        IF ItemG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" <> '' THEN
          "VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" := ItemG."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)";
        IF ItemG."Inventory Posting Group" <> '' THEN
          "Inventory Posting Group" := ItemG."Inventory Posting Group";
        IF ItemG."Model Year" <> '' THEN
          "Model Year" := ItemG."Model Year";
        IF ItemG."Top Speed" <> 0 THEN
          "Top Speed" := ItemG."Top Speed";
        IF ItemG.Acceleration <> 0 THEN
          Acceleration := ItemG.Acceleration;
        IF ItemG."Tariff No." <> '' THEN
          "Tariff No." := ItemG."Tariff No.";
        IF ItemG."National Tariff No." <> '' THEN
          "National Tariff No." := ItemG."National Tariff No.";
        IF ItemG."Country of Origin Code" <> '' THEN
          "Country of Origin Code" := ItemG."Country of Origin Code";
      // Start PA039505
        IF ItemG."No. of Seats" <> 0 THEN
          "No. of Seats" := ItemG."No. of Seats";
      // Stop PA039505
      // Start PA035258
        Drive := ItemG.Drive;
      // Stop PA035258
      // Start PA033043
        "Diesel Particulate Filter" := ItemG."Diesel Particulate Filter";
      // Stop PA033043
      // Start PA038140.42926

    PROCEDURE DefineOption@5();
    VAR
      VehicleOptionL@1109400000 : Record 5025422;
    BEGIN
      VehicleOptionL.RESET;
      VehicleOptionL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
      VehicleOptionL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF VehicleOptionL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        IF VehicleOptionL.COUNT = 1 THEN BEGIN
          VehicleOptionL.DELETE;
          IF "Model No." <> '' THEN
            VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateVehicleOption(Rec);
        END ELSE BEGIN
      // Start PA032651
          IF NOT GUIALLOWED OR NOT VehicleG.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA032651
            VehicleOptionL.DELETEALL;
            IF "Model No." <> '' THEN
              VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateVehicleOption(Rec);
          END ELSE
      // Start PA033155
            IF NOT VehicleInsertG THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA033155
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC011, FALSE) THEN BEGIN
                VehicleOptionL.DELETEALL;
                IF "Model No." <> '' THEN
                  VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateVehicleOption(Rec);
              END ELSE
                ERROR(C_INC012, FIELDCAPTION("Model No."));
      // Start PA033155
            END ELSE BEGIN
              VehicleOptionL.DELETEALL;
              IF "Model No." <> '' THEN
                VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateVehicleOption(Rec);
            END;
      // Stop PA033155
        END;
      END ELSE
        IF "Model No." <> '' THEN
          VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateVehicleOption(Rec);
      VehicleCollectionUnitG.CreateNewPriceSticker(Rec, VehicleCollectionUnitG.ReturnManual());
    END;

    PROCEDURE ChangeSalesPrices@7();
    VAR
      NewVATPercentL@1109400000 : Decimal;
      DifferencialTaxL@1109400001 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF ("VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" <> xRec."VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)") OR
         ("VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> xRec."VAT Prod. Posting Group")
      THEN BEGIN
        IF ("VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)" <> '') AND ("VAT Prod. Posting Group" <> '') THEN BEGIN
          IF NOT VATPostingSetupG.GET("VAT Bus. Posting Gr. (Price)", "VAT Prod. Posting Group") THEN
            VATPostingSetupG.INIT;
          CASE VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type" OF
            VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT":
              VATPostingSetupG."VAT %" := 0;
          END;

          NewVATPercentL := VATPostingSetupG."VAT %";
          IF VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type" = VATPostingSetupG."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
            DifferencialTaxL := TRUE
          ELSE
            DifferencialTaxL := FALSE;

        END ELSE BEGIN
          NewVATPercentL := 0;
          DifferencialTaxL := FALSE;
        END;

        VehicleOptionG.RESET;
        VehicleOptionG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
        IF VehicleOptionG.FINDSET(TRUE) THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            VehicleOptionG.SalesAmountVATChange(NewVATPercentL, DifferencialTaxL);
            VehicleOptionG.MODIFY;
          UNTIL VehicleOptionG.NEXT = 0;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AutomPullVIN@15();
    VAR
      RecL@19176600 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // @ Pull VIN from range of nos. with check for uniqueness across all companies
      VehicleSetupG.TESTFIELD("Vehicle Nos.");
      CompanyG.RESET;
      // Start EU.0191766
      CompanyG.SETFILTER(Name, '<>%1', CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      FoundInOtherCompanyG := FALSE;
      REPEAT
        VIN := '';
        NoSeriesMgtG.InitSeries(VehicleSetupG."Vehicle Nos.", xRec."No. Series", 0D, VIN, "No. Series");
        IF CompanyG.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
      // Start PA041093.65483
      // Start EU.0191766
            IF HasAccessControl() THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA041093.65483
              RecL.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyG.Name);
              FoundInOtherCompanyG := RecL.GET(VIN);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Start PA041093.65483
            END;
      // Stop PA041093.65483
          UNTIL (CompanyG.NEXT = 0) OR FoundInOtherCompanyG;
      UNTIL NOT FoundInOtherCompanyG;
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchVinExists@6(VAR VinP@13279501 : Code[20];ExVinP@13279502 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      VehicleL@1000 : Record 5025400;
      TempVehicleL@13279503 : TEMPORARY Record 5025400;
      NewVinL@1001 : Text;
      SearchFromPosL@14391400 : Integer;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0126935.127489
      // Start EU.0129713.132549
      IF VinP > '' THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0143914.144319
        VehicleSetupG.GET();
        CASE VehicleSetupG."Unique Veh. Identifc. from VIN" OF
          VehicleSetupG."Unique Veh. Identifc. from VIN"::"Last 7 VIN Chars":
            SearchFromPosL := 7;
          VehicleSetupG."Unique Veh. Identifc. from VIN"::"Last 8 VIN Chars":
            SearchFromPosL := 8;
          VehicleSetupG."Unique Veh. Identifc. from VIN"::"Last 9 VIN Chars":
            SearchFromPosL := 9;
          VehicleSetupG."Unique Veh. Identifc. from VIN"::"Last 10 VIN Chars":
            SearchFromPosL := 10;
        END;
        IF SearchFromPosL = 0 THEN
          VehicleL.SETFILTER(VIN,VinP)
        ELSE
          IF STRLEN(VinP) <= SearchFromPosL THEN
      // Stop EU.0143914.144319
            VehicleL.SETFILTER(VIN, '*' + VinP)
          ELSE
      // Start EU.0143914.144319
            VehicleL.SETFILTER(VIN, '*' + COPYSTR(VinP, STRLEN(VinP) - SearchFromPosL + 1));
      // Stop  EU.0143914.144319
        IF VehicleL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            IF VehicleL.VIN <> ExVinP THEN BEGIN
              TempVehicleL := VehicleL;
              TempVehicleL.INSERT;
            END;
          UNTIL VehicleL.NEXT = 0;
        VehicleL.RESET;
        NewVinL := VinP;
        IF NOT TempVehicleL.FINDFIRST THEN
          WHILE NewVinL > '' DO
            IF STRPOS('1234567890ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPRQSTUVWXYZ', COPYSTR(NewVinL, 1, 1)) = 0 THEN
              ERROR(C_INC_NewVinContainsWrongCharacters, COPYSTR(NewVinL, 1, 1))
            ELSE
              NewVinL := COPYSTR(NewVinL, 2)
        ELSE BEGIN
          VehicleL.GET(TempVehicleL.VIN);
          VehicleL.CALCFIELDS(Name);
          ERROR(C_INC_VehicleAlreadyExist, STRSUBSTNO('(%1 %2, %3)', VehicleL.VIN, VehicleL."License No.", VehicleL.Name));
        END
      END;
      // Stop EU.0129713.132549
      // Stop EU.0126935.127489
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchVehicleOverAllCompanies@9(OptionsP@1109400000 : Text[30]);
    VAR
      OtherRecL@19176601 : Record 5025400;
      AddressSetupL@12016100 : Record 5029113;
      LatestVehicleTmpL@117502 : Record 5025400;
      ServCampAffectedVehL@18884300 : Record 5025571;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0120161.119211
      AddressSetupL.GET();
      IF NOT AddressSetupL."Update All Companies" THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop EU.0120161.119211
      // Start EU.0188843.188665
      IF STRPOS(OptionsP,'/VEHICLE-CHANGE') > 0 THEN BEGIN
        ServCampAffectedVehL.SETRANGE(VIN,VIN);
        IF ServCampAffectedVehL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            IF ServCampAffectedVehL.FillFieldsfromVehicle(Rec) THEN
              ServCampAffectedVehL.MODIFY(TRUE);
          UNTIL ServCampAffectedVehL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0188843.188665
      CompanyG.RESET;
      IF CompanyG.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA041093.65483
      // Start EU.0191766
          IF HasAccessControl() THEN
      // Stop PA041093.65483
            IF CompanyG.Name <> CURRENTCOMPANY THEN BEGIN
              OtherRecL.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyG.Name);
              IF OtherRecL.GET(VIN) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Start PA033669
                IF STRPOS(OptionsP, '/PURCHASE-CHECK') > 0 THEN
                  NewVehicleFromOtherCompanyG := TRUE;
      // Stop PA033669
                // Synchronize Veh. Data
                IF STRPOS(OptionsP,'/VEHICLE-CHANGE') > 0 THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0004569
      // Start EU.0191766
                  VehicleCustIsPrivateG := NOT AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(OtherRecL."Address No.",FALSE, CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0004569
                  CopyVehicleFields(Rec, OtherRecL, FALSE, VehicleCustIsPrivateG);
                  OtherRecL.MODIFY;
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Start EU.0188843.188665
                  ServCampAffectedVehL.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyG.Name);
                  ServCampAffectedVehL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
                  IF ServCampAffectedVehL.FINDSET THEN
                    REPEAT
                      IF ServCampAffectedVehL.FillFieldsfromVehicle(Rec) THEN
                        ServCampAffectedVehL.MODIFY(TRUE);
                    UNTIL ServCampAffectedVehL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop EU.0188843.188665
                END;
      // Start PA040256.58691
                IF STRPOS(OptionsP, '/CHECK-COMPANIES') > 0 THEN
                  VehicleExistOtherCompanyG := TRUE;
      // Stop PA040256.58691

                // Create vehicle of other company in the current company
      // Start EU.0001175.6097
      // Start EU.0191766
                IF STRPOS(OptionsP, '/VEHICLE-INSERT') > 0 THEN BEGIN
                  // Search for the vehicle with latest 'Last Date Modified'
                  IF OtherRecL."Last Date Modified" >= LatestVehicleTmpL."Last Date Modified" THEN BEGIN
                    LatestVehicleTmpL.CHANGECOMPANY(CompanyG.Name);
                    LatestVehicleTmpL := OtherRecL;
                  END;
                END;
      // Start PA041093.65483
              END;
            END;
      // Stop PA041093.65483
        UNTIL CompanyG.NEXT = 0;

      IF STRPOS(OptionsP, '/VEHICLE-INSERT') > 0 THEN
        IF LatestVehicleTmpL.VIN <> '' THEN BEGIN
          OtherRecL.RESET;
          OtherRecL.CHANGECOMPANY(LatestVehicleTmpL.CURRENTCOMPANY);
          OtherRecL.GET(LatestVehicleTmpL.VIN);
          CheckCustomerProspectData(OtherRecL, VehicleCustIsPrivateG);
          VehicleCompanyChange(OtherRecL, LatestVehicleTmpL.CURRENTCOMPANY, Rec);
        END;
        // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0001175.6097
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehicleCompanyChange@14(VAR SourceVehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400;SourceCompanyP@1109400001 : Text[30];VAR TargetVehicleP@1109400002 : Record 5025400);
    VAR
      AddressL@1109400003 : Record 5029111;
      FromOptionL@1109400004 : Record 5025422;
      ToOptionL@1109400005 : Record 5025422;
      FromModelL@1109400006 : Record 27;
      ToModelL@19176604 : Record 27;
      FromCommentLineL@1109400007 : Record 5028653;
      ToCommentLineL@1109400008 : Record 5028653;
      FromMakeL@1109400009 : Record 12;
      ToMakeL@19176605 : Record 12;
      FromVehApptL@1109400010 : Record 5025450;
      ToVehApptL@1109400011 : Record 5025450;
      FromRemarkL@1109400012 : Record 5028654;
      ToRemarkL@1109400013 : Record 5028654;
      FromEngineDiagDataL@1109400014 : Record 5025407;
      ToEngineDiagDataL@1109400015 : Record 5025407;
      FromCustFinancingL@1109400016 : Record 5025429;
      ToCustFinancingL@19176600 : Record 5025429;
      FromVehicleInsuranceL@1109400017 : Record 5025430;
      FromVehicleCustL@1109400018 : Record 5025469;
      ToVehicleCustL@1109400019 : Record 5025469;
      FromCustL@1109400020 : Record 18;
      ToCustL@1109400021 : Record 18;
      FromProtectedVehCodeL@1109400022 : Record 5045458;
      ToProtectedVehCodeL@1109400023 : Record 5045458;
      FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL@1109400024 : Record 5045457;
      ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL@1109400025 : Record 5045457;
      FromContactL@1101140603 : Record 5050;
      ToContactL@1101140604 : Record 5050;
      FromTechDataValueL@1109400027 : Record 5205856;
      ToTechDataValueL@1109400028 : Record 5205856;
      FromTechDataDescrL@1109400031 : Record 5205852;
      ToTechDataDescrL@1109400032 : Record 5205852;
      SkipRecInsertL@19176603 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function transfers the fields of a vehicle record from a
      // @ other companies to the current company.  Only new
      VehicleFromOtherCompanyG := FALSE;
      ModelFromOtherCompanyG := FALSE;
      // Start PA042533
      VehicleOptionsFromOtherCompanyG := FALSE;
      // Stop PA042533
      // Start PA042760
      TargetVehicleP.INIT;
      TargetVehicleP."Vehicle Status" := SourceVehicleP."Vehicle Status";
      // Stop PA042760
      TargetVehicleP.VIN := SourceVehicleP.VIN;
      TargetVehicleP.INSERT;
      VehicleFromOtherCompanyG := TRUE;

      // Start PA042539.85419
      // Transfer make
      // Start EU.0191766
      ToMakeL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromMakeL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      IF NOT ToMakeL.GET(SourceVehicleP."Make Code") THEN
        IF FromMakeL.GET(SourceVehicleP."Make Code") THEN BEGIN
          ToMakeL := FromMakeL;
          ToMakeL.INSERT(TRUE);
        END;
      // Stop PA042539.85419

      ToCustL.RESET;
      ToCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      ToContactL.RESET;
      ToContactL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      CopyVehicleFields(SourceVehicleP, TargetVehicleP, TRUE, VehicleCustIsPrivateG);
      ToCustL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
      ToCustL.SETRANGE("Address No.", SourceVehicleP."Address No.");
      IF ToCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        TargetVehicleP."Customer No." := ToCustL."No.";
        ToContactL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
        ToContactL.SETRANGE("Address No.", ToCustL."Address No.");
        ToContactL.SETRANGE("Customer No.", ToCustL."No.");
        ToContactL.SETRANGE(Type, ToContactL.Type::Company);
        IF ToContactL.FINDFIRST THEN
          TargetVehicleP."Contact No." := ToContactL."No.";
      END;
      // Start PA042760
      // Prospect Vehicle
      ToContactL.RESET;
      ToContactL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      IF TargetVehicleP."Vehicle Status" = SourceVehicleP."Vehicle Status"::"Prospect Vehicle" THEN BEGIN
        TargetVehicleP.SETRANGE("Address No.", SourceVehicleP."Address No.");
        ToContactL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
        ToContactL.SETRANGE("Address No.", SourceVehicleP."Address No.");
        ToContactL.SETRANGE(Type, ToContactL.Type::Company);
      // Start EU.0004569
        IF ToContactL.FINDFIRST AND
           AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(SourceVehicleP."Address No.",FALSE,SourceCompanyP)
      // Stop EU.0004569
        THEN
          TargetVehicleP."Contact No." := ToContactL."No.";
      // Stop EU.0191766
      END;
      // Stop PA042760
      ToCustL.RESET;
      ToCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromCustL.RESET;
      FromCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      IF SourceVehicleP."Old Customer No." > '' THEN BEGIN
        FromCustL.GET(SourceVehicleP."Old Customer No.");
        ToCustL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
        ToCustL.SETRANGE("Address No.", FromCustL."Address No.");
      // Stop EU.0191766
        IF ToCustL.FINDFIRST THEN
          TargetVehicleP."Old Customer No." := ToCustL."No.";
      END;
      // Start EU.0004569
      // Start EU.0191766
      IF AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(SourceVehicleP."Address No.",FALSE,SourceCompanyP) THEN
      // Stop EU.0191766
        TargetVehicleP."Address No." := SourceVehicleP."Address No.";
      // Stop EU.0004569
      TargetVehicleP.MODIFY;

      // Start PA042539.85419
      // Stop PA042539.85419

      // Transfer Veh. Model.
      // Start EU.0191766
      ToModelL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromModelL.RESET;
      FromModelL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      IF NOT ToModelL.GET(TargetVehicleP."Model No.") THEN
        IF FromModelL.GET(TargetVehicleP."Model No.") THEN BEGIN
          ToModelL := FromModelL;
          ToModelL.INSERT(TRUE);
          ModelFromOtherCompanyG := TRUE;
        END;

      ToOptionL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      ToModelL.RESET;
      ToModelL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      IF (TargetVehicleP."Model No." > '') AND
         ToModelL.GET(TargetVehicleP."Model No.") AND
         (ToModelL."Item Type" = ToModelL."Item Type"::Vehicle) AND
         (ToModelL."Make Code" = TargetVehicleP."Make Code")
      THEN BEGIN
        TargetVehicleP.VALIDATE("Model No.");
      // Stop EU.0191766
        ToOptionL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
        IF NOT ToOptionL.ISEMPTY THEN
          ToOptionL.DELETEALL;
      END;

      // Transfer vehicle options as well (copy only texts)
      FromOptionL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromOptionL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromOptionL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0191766
        REPEAT
          ToOptionL := FromOptionL;
      // Stop EU.0191766
          ToOptionL.INSERT;
        UNTIL FromOptionL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start PA042533
        VehicleOptionsFromOtherCompanyG := TRUE;
      // Stop PA042533
      END;
      ToOptionL.UpdateArchiv(0, TRUE, ToOptionL.ReturnManual);

      // Transfer Protected Code Texts
      // Start EU.0191766
      ToProtectedVehCodeL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromProtectedVehCodeL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromProtectedVehCodeL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromProtectedVehCodeL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ToProtectedVehCodeL := FromProtectedVehCodeL;
          IF NOT ToProtectedVehCodeL.GET(ToProtectedVehCodeL.RECORDID) THEN
            ToProtectedVehCodeL.INSERT;
          // Transfer Protected Vehicle Code Type
          ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
          FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
          FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL.SETRANGE("Make Code", FromProtectedVehCodeL."Make Code");
          FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL.SETRANGE(Code, FromProtectedVehCodeL.Code);
          IF FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL := FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL;
              IF NOT ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL.GET(ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL.RECORDID) THEN BEGIN
                ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL := FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL;
                ToProtectedVehCodeTypeL.INSERT;
              END;
            UNTIL FromProtectedVehCodeTypeL.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL FromProtectedVehCodeL.NEXT = 0;

      // Copy comment lines
      ToCommentLineL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromCommentLineL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromCommentLineL.SETRANGE("Table Name", FromCommentLineL."Table Name"::Vehicle);
      FromCommentLineL.SETRANGE("No.", TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromCommentLineL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        ToCommentLineL.SETRANGE("Table Name", ToCommentLineL."Table Name"::Vehicle);
        ToCommentLineL.SETRANGE("No.", TargetVehicleP.VIN);
        ToCommentLineL.DELETEALL;
        REPEAT
      // Stop EU.0191766
          ToCommentLineL := FromCommentLineL;
          ToCommentLineL.INSERT;
        UNTIL FromCommentLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      // Copy vehicle appointment types
      FromVehApptL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromVehApptL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromVehApptL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA034051
      // Start EU.0191766
          FromVehApptL.CompanyDataTransfer(FromVehApptL, TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop PA034051
        UNTIL FromVehApptL.NEXT = 0;

      // Copy remarks
      FromRemarkL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromRemarkL.SETRANGE("Table Name", FromRemarkL."Table Name"::Vehicle);
      FromRemarkL.SETRANGE("No.", TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      // Start EU.0191766
      ToRemarkL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      IF FromRemarkL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        ToRemarkL.SETRANGE("Table Name", ToRemarkL."Table Name"::Vehicle);
        ToRemarkL.SETRANGE("No.", TargetVehicleP.VIN);
        ToRemarkL.DELETEALL;
        REPEAT
          ToRemarkL := FromRemarkL;
          ToRemarkL.INSERT;
        UNTIL FromRemarkL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Copy Engine Diagnostic Data
      ToEngineDiagDataL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      FromEngineDiagDataL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromEngineDiagDataL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromEngineDiagDataL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start EU.0191766
          ToEngineDiagDataL := FromEngineDiagDataL;
          IF NOT ToEngineDiagDataL.GET(ToEngineDiagDataL.RECORDID) THEN BEGIN
            ToEngineDiagDataL."Order No." := '';
            ToEngineDiagDataL.INSERT;
          END;
        UNTIL FromEngineDiagDataL.NEXT = 0;

      // Transfer customer financing (only latest record)
      FromCustFinancingL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromCustFinancingL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromCustFinancingL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
        SkipRecInsertL := FALSE;
        ToCustFinancingL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
        ToCustFinancingL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
        FromCustFinancingL."Line No." := 0;
        IF ToCustFinancingL.FINDLAST THEN BEGIN
          FromCustFinancingL."Line No." := ToCustFinancingL."Line No.";
          SkipRecInsertL := FORMAT(FromCustFinancingL) = FORMAT(ToCustFinancingL);
        END;
        IF NOT SkipRecInsertL THEN BEGIN
          ToCustFinancingL := FromCustFinancingL;
          ToCustFinancingL."Line No." += 10000;
          ToCustFinancingL.INSERT;
        END;
      END;

      // Copy all vehicle insurance records
      FromVehicleInsuranceL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromVehicleInsuranceL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      IF FromVehicleInsuranceL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          FromVehicleInsuranceL.CompanyDataTransfer(FromVehicleInsuranceL, TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
        UNTIL FromVehicleInsuranceL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop EU.0191766

      // Transfer Ve. Customers
      ToCustL.RESET;
      FromCustL.RESET;
      ToContactL.RESET;
      FromContactL.RESET;
      ToCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      ToVehicleCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      ToContactL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      FromVehicleCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      // Start PA036398
      FromContactL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      FromVehicleCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      // Start PA042539.85419
      FromCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      // Stop PA042539.85419
      IF FromVehicleCustL.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        ToCustL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
        REPEAT
      // Start EU.0191766
          CLEAR(ToContactL);
          IF FromContactL.GET(FromVehicleCustL."Contact No.") AND
      // Start EU.0004569
            AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(FromContactL."Address No.",FALSE,SourceCompanyP)
          THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0004569
            ToContactL.SETRANGE("Address No.",FromContactL."Address No.");
            IF NOT ToContactL.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
              AddressL.GET(FromContactL."Address No.");
      // Start EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.DEF(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.MakeProspect(AddressL);
              ToContactL.FINDFIRST;
            END;
            IF (ToContactL."Customer No." = '') AND (FromVehicleCustL."Customer No." <> '') THEN BEGIN
      // Start PA042539.85419
              FromCustL.GET(FromVehicleCustL."Customer No.");
              ToCustL := FromCustL;
      // Stop PA042539.85419
              ToCustL."No." := '';
              ToCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
              AddressL.GET(FromContactL."Address No.");
      // Start EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.DEF(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.ChangeCustomer(ToCustL, AddressL);
      // Start PA042539.85419
              ToContactL.FINDFIRST;
      // Stop PA042539.85419
            END;
      // Start EU.0004569
      // Start EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0004569
          END;
          ToVehicleCustL := FromVehicleCustL;
          ToVehicleCustL."Customer No." := ToContactL."Customer No.";
          ToVehicleCustL."Contact No." := ToContactL."No.";

          IF (FromVehicleCustL."Contact Person No." <> '') AND FromContactL.GET(FromVehicleCustL."Contact Person No.") THEN BEGIN
            ToContactL.SETRANGE("Address No.",FromContactL."Address No.");
      // Start EU.0004569
      // Start EU.0191766
            IF NOT ToContactL.FIND('-') AND AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(FromContactL."Address No.",FALSE,SourceCompanyP) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0191766
      // Stop EU.0004569
              AddressL.GET(FromContactL."Address No.");
              ToContactL."No." := '';
              ToContactL.Type := ToContactL.Type::Person;
              ToContactL."Company No." := ToVehicleCustL."Contact No.";
              ToContactL.INSERT(TRUE);
      // Start EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.DEF(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Stop EU.0191766
              AddressMgntG.InsertContactInfo(ToContactL, AddressL);
      // Start PA036398.30880
              ToContactL.MODIFY;
      // Stop PA036398.30880
            END;
            ToVehicleCustL."Contact Person No." := ToContactL."No.";
          END;
      // Stop PA036398
      // Start EU.0004569
      // Start EU.0156444.158128
      // Stop EU.0156444.158128
      // Stop EU.0004569
          ToVehicleCustL.INSERT;
        UNTIL FromVehicleCustL.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      // Start EU.0020651
      // Start EU.0027334
      // Stop EU.0027334
      // Start EU.0191766
      // Start EU.0027334
      // Stop EU.0191766
      FromTechDataDescrL.RESET;
      // Stop EU.0027334
      FromTechDataDescrL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);

      // Start EU.0027334
      // Stop EU.0027334
      FromTechDataValueL.RESET;
      // Start EU.0027334
      FromTechDataValueL.CHANGECOMPANY(SourceCompanyP);
      // Stop EU.0027334
      // Start EU.0191766
      ToTechDataValueL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      ToTechDataDescrL.CHANGECOMPANY(TargetVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      FromTechDataValueL.SETRANGE("Record Id", SourceVehicleP.RECORDID);
      // Stop EU.0191766
      IF NOT FromTechDataValueL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
        FromTechDataValueL.FINDSET;
        REPEAT
          ToTechDataValueL := FromTechDataValueL;
          ToTechDataValueL.SETCURRENTKEY("Layer Code", "Requirement Code",
            "Record Id", "Technical Data Code");
          ToTechDataValueL.SETRECFILTER;
          ToTechDataValueL.SETRANGE("Entry No.");
          IF ToTechDataValueL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
            ToTechDataValueL."Entry No." := 0;
            ToTechDataValueL.INSERT(TRUE);

            FromTechDataDescrL.RESET;
            FromTechDataDescrL.SETRANGE("Layer Code", FromTechDataValueL."Layer Code");
            FromTechDataDescrL.SETRANGE("Requirement Code", FromTechDataValueL."Requirement Code");
            FromTechDataDescrL.SETRANGE("Technical Data Code", FromTechDataValueL."Technical Data Code");
            IF NOT FromTechDataDescrL.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN
              FromTechDataDescrL.FINDSET;
              REPEAT
      // Start EU.0191766
                ToTechDataDescrL := FromTechDataDescrL;
                IF NOT ToTechDataDescrL.GET(ToTechDataDescrL.RECORDID) THEN
                  ToTechDataValueL.INSERT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0191766
              UNTIL FromTechDataDescrL.NEXT = 0;
            END;
          END;
        UNTIL FromTechDataValueL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0020651
      // Start EU.0191766
      TargetVehicleP.GET(TargetVehicleP.VIN);
      // Stop EU.0191766
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CopyVehicleFields@12(VAR FromVehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400;VAR ToVehicleP@1109400001 : Record 5025400;InsertP@1109400002 : Boolean;VehicleCustIsPrivateP@19176601 : Boolean);
    VAR
      VehicleSetupL@19176600 : Record 5025401;
      GenProdPostGroupL@1109400003 : Record 251;
      ContactL@15236400 : Record 5050;
      CustomerL@15236401 : Record 18;
    BEGIN
      // Start EU.0191766
      VehicleSetupL.CHANGECOMPANY(ToVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      GenProdPostGroupL.CHANGECOMPANY(ToVehicleP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      VehicleSetupL.GET;
      // Start EU.0004569
      IF NOT VehicleCustIsPrivateP THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0191766
        ToVehicleP."License No." := FromVehicleP."License No.";
