      // Start EU.0195242
      OnAfterCopyVehicleFieldsEvent(FromVehicleP, ToVehicleP, InsertP, VehicleCustIsPrivateP);
      // Stop EU.0195242
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeleteAddtlTables@10();
    VAR
      VehicleCodesL@1109400000 : Record 5045458;
      VehicleServContractL@1115000000 : Record 5061005;
      ServCampNegVehL@1101314645 : Record 5025699;
      ServCampainAffectedVehL@1101314646 : Record 5025571;
      VehicleWarrL@1101140603 : Record 5025465;
    BEGIN
      CommentLineG.RESET;
      CommentLineG.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineG."Table Name"::Vehicle);
      CommentLineG.SETRANGE("No.", VIN);
      CommentLineG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      OptionG.RESET;
      OptionG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      OptionG.DELETEALL;
      // Start PA036997
      VehOptionBOMG.RESET;
      VehOptionBOMG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF NOT VehOptionBOMG.ISEMPTY THEN
        VehOptionBOMG.DELETEALL;
      // Stop PA036997
      EngineDiagnosticDataG.RESET;
      EngineDiagnosticDataG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      EngineDiagnosticDataG.DELETEALL;
      EvaluationG.RESET;
      EvaluationG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      EvaluationG.DELETEALL;
      CustFinancingG.RESET;
      CustFinancingG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      CustFinancingG.DELETEALL;
      VehicleInsuranceG.RESET;
      VehicleInsuranceG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      VehicleInsuranceG.DELETEALL;
      VehicleRemarkG.RESET;
      VehicleRemarkG.SETRANGE("Table Name", VehicleRemarkG."Table Name"::Vehicle);
      VehicleRemarkG.SETRANGE("No.", VIN);
      VehicleRemarkG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      PurchFinancingG.RESET;
      PurchFinancingG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      PurchFinancingG.DELETEALL;
      VehCustG.RESET;
      VehCustG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      // Start PA036398
      // Stop PA036398
      IF VehCustG.FINDFIRST THEN
        REPEAT
      // Start PA036398
          IF VehCustG.Type = VehCustG.Type::"Factory Warranty" THEN BEGIN
            VehicleWarrL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
            VehicleWarrL.DELETEALL;
          END;
          VehCustG.DELETE();
      // Stop PA036398
        UNTIL VehCustG.NEXT = 0;
      VehApptG.RESET;
      VehApptG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      VehApptG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      VehiclePriceStickerG.RESET;
      VehiclePriceStickerG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      VehiclePriceStickerG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      VehicleCodesL.RESET;
      VehicleCodesL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      VehicleCodesL.DELETEALL;
      // Start PA032461
      // Stop PA032461
      // Start PA032500
      VehicleServContractL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      VehicleServContractL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032500
      // Start PA032812
      VehicleDealerStatusHistoryG.RESET;
      VehicleDealerStatusHistoryG.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF NOT VehicleDealerStatusHistoryG.ISEMPTY THEN
        VehicleDealerStatusHistoryG.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      // Stop PA032812
      // Start PA034598
      ServCampainAffectedVehL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
      ServCampainAffectedVehL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF NOT ServCampainAffectedVehL.ISEMPTY THEN
        ServCampainAffectedVehL.DELETEALL(TRUE);
      // Stop PA034598
      // Start PA034598.I001660
      ServCampNegVehL.DeleteVIN(VIN);
      // Stop PA034598.I001660
    END;

    PROCEDURE SetVehicleWarranty@11();
    VAR
      WarrSetupL@1109400000 : Record 5025466;
      VehicleWarrL@1109400001 : Record 5025465;
      VehicleCustL@1109400002 : Record 5025469;
      DateFormulaL@1109400003 : Text[30];
    BEGIN
      // Start IMM27064
      IF ("Initial Registration" <> 0D) OR (IsImporter AND ("Customer Registration Date" <> 0D)) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop IMM27064
        VehicleWarrL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
        VehicleWarrL.DELETEALL;
        WarrSetupL.SETRANGE("Make Code", "Make Code");
        WarrSetupL.SETRANGE("Vehicle Category Code", "Vehicle Category Code");
      // Start IMM27064
        IF IsImporter THEN
          WarrSetupL.SETRANGE("Warranty Optional", FALSE);
      // Stop IMM27064
        IF WarrSetupL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          REPEAT
            VehicleWarrL.INIT;
            VehicleWarrL.VIN := VIN;
            VehicleWarrL."Warranty Type" := WarrSetupL."Warranty Type";
      // Start IMM27064
            IF (NOT IsImporter) OR (WarrSetupL."Warranty Start Date" = WarrSetupL."Warranty Start Date"::"Initial Registration Date") THEN
              VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract" := "Initial Registration"
            ELSE
              VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract" := "Customer Registration Date";
            IF VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract" <> 0D THEN BEGIN
              CASE WarrSetupL."Warranty Unit of Measure" OF
                WarrSetupL."Warranty Unit of Measure"::Day:
                  DateFormulaL := '<+%1D>';
                WarrSetupL."Warranty Unit of Measure"::Month:
                  DateFormulaL := '<+%1M>';
                WarrSetupL."Warranty Unit of Measure"::Year:
                  DateFormulaL := '<+%1Y>';
              END;
      // Start IMM27064
              VehicleWarrL."Expiration of Contract" := CALCDATE(STRSUBSTNO(DateFormulaL, WarrSetupL."Warranty Term"), VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract");
      // Stop IMM27064
              VehicleWarrL."Labor Price Group" := WarrSetupL."Labor Price Group";
              VehicleWarrL."Ext. Service Price Group" := WarrSetupL."Ext. Service Price Group";
              VehicleWarrL."Item Sales Price Group" := WarrSetupL."Item Sales Price Group";
              VehicleWarrL."max. Mileage" := WarrSetupL."max. Mileage";
              IF (WarrSetupL."Valid from" = 0D) OR
                 (WarrSetupL."Valid from" >= VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract") AND
                 (WarrSetupL."Valid to" = 0D) OR (VehicleWarrL."Beginning of Contract" <= WarrSetupL."Valid to") AND
                 ((WarrSetupL."max. Mileage" = 0) OR
                 (Mileage <= WarrSetupL."max. Mileage"))
              THEN
                VehicleWarrL.INSERT;
            END;
      // Stop IMM27064
          UNTIL WarrSetupL.NEXT = 0;
          VehicleCustL.RESET;
          VehicleCustL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
          VehicleCustL.SETRANGE(Type, VehicleCustL.Type::"Factory Warranty");
          IF NOT VehicleCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            VehicleCustL.INIT;
            VehicleCustL.VIN := VIN;
            VehicleCustL.VALIDATE(Type, VehicleCustL.Type::"Factory Warranty");
            VehicleCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
          END;
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE WarrantyWithOwnSalesVehicleCheck@1055604(VINP@1055600 : Code[20];BillToCustomerNoP@1055602 : Code[20];MakeCodeP@1055603 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      RecL@1055601 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // @ Function will check, if a vehicle was sold by the current dealer and if the planned BillToCustomer is a Warranty Customer.
      // Start EU.0054980
      IF BillToCustomerNoP > '' THEN
        IF VINP > '' THEN BEGIN
          IF VINP = VIN THEN
            RecL := Rec
          ELSE
            IF NOT RecL.GET(VINP) THEN
              EXIT(FALSE);
          IF MakeCodeP = '' THEN
            MakeCodeP := RecL."Make Code";
          IF MakeCodeP > '' THEN
            IF RecL."Own Sale" OR (RecL."Vehicle Status" IN [RecL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle", RecL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle"]) THEN BEGIN
              IF MakeSetupG."Make Code" <> MakeCodeP THEN
                IF NOT MakeSetupG.GET(MakeCodeP) THEN
                  EXIT(FALSE);
              IF MakeSetupG."Tax-Exempt Own Sales Warranty" THEN BEGIN
                IF MakeG.Code <> MakeCodeP THEN
                  IF NOT MakeG.GET(MakeCodeP) THEN
                    EXIT(FALSE);
                EXIT(MakeG."Factory Warranty Customer" = BillToCustomerNoP);
              END;
            END;
        END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop EU.0054980
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehicleSearch@13(SearchVINP@1109400000 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      SearchVehicleL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA032636
      EXIT(VehicleSearchPrefiltered(SearchVINP, SearchVehicleL, TRUE));
      // Stop PA032636
    END;

    PROCEDURE VehicleSearchPrefiltered@1109400011(SearchVINP@1109400000 : Code[20];VAR SearchVehicleP@1109400001 : Record 5025400;AcceptNonExistingVINP@1109400002 : Boolean) : Code[20];
    VAR
      SkipTriggerExecutionL@19881800 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function is used for performing a vehicle search. It is called from multiple places. E.g. the VIN Field in the
      // @ Service Order. It will try to find a vehicle the following way
      // @ 1) GET with the full VIN
      // @ 2) Filter on the Search Description
      // @ 3) Filter with the Backwards String of the SearchCriteria on the "VIN Check Code"
      // @ If in case 2) or 3) multiple records apply, a selection window will be shown
      // @ param SearchVINP The search criterion. Can either be a VIN or a License Plate No.
      // @ retval the VIN of the found Vehicle
      // Start EU.0198818.199111
      OnBeforeVehicleSearchPrefilteredEvent(SearchVehicleP, SearchVINP,SkipTriggerExecutionL);
      IF SkipTriggerExecutionL THEN
        EXIT;
      // Stop EU.0198818.199111
      // Start PA032636
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE(VIN, SearchVINP);
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDFIRST THEN
        EXIT(SearchVINP);
      SearchVehicleP.SETFILTER(VIN, SearchVINP + '*');
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SearchVehicleP.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL SearchVehicleP.NEXT = 0;
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE(VIN);
      SearchVehicleP.SETCURRENTKEY("Search Description");
      SearchVehicleP.SETFILTER("Search Description", SearchVINP + '*');
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SearchVehicleP.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL SearchVehicleP.NEXT = 0;
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE("Search Description");
      // Start PA042349
      // Start EU.0000497
      SearchVehicleP.SETFILTER("License No. Compressed", CompressLicenseNo(SearchVINP) + '*');
      // Stop EU.0000497
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SearchVehicleP.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL SearchVehicleP.NEXT = 0;
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE("License No. Compressed");
      // Stop PA042349
      // Start EU.0000044
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE("License No. Compressed");
      SearchVehicleP.SETFILTER("License No. Check Code", CollectionUnitG.BackString(SearchVINP) + '*');
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SearchVehicleP.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL SearchVehicleP.NEXT = 0;
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE("License No. Check Code");
      // Stop EU.0000044
      SearchVehicleP.SETCURRENTKEY("VIN Check Code");
      SearchVehicleP.SETFILTER("VIN Check Code", CollectionUnitG.BackString(SearchVINP) + '*');
      IF SearchVehicleP.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SearchVehicleP.MARK(TRUE);
        UNTIL SearchVehicleP.NEXT = 0;
      SearchVehicleP.SETRANGE("VIN Check Code");
      SearchVehicleP.SETCURRENTKEY("Search Description");
      SearchVehicleP.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
      IF NOT SearchVehicleP.FINDFIRST THEN
        EXIT(SearchVINP);
      // Start EU.0145355.143028
      // Stop EU.0145355.143028
      IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(PAGE::"Vehicle List", SearchVehicleP) <> ACTION::LookupOK THEN
        IF AcceptNonExistingVINP THEN
          EXIT(SearchVINP)
        ELSE
          ERROR('');
      EXIT(SearchVehicleP.VIN);
      // Stop PA032636
    END;

    PROCEDURE FieldValue@16(VehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400;FieldP@1109400001 : Integer;SourceP@1109400002 : ' ,Service,Vehicle Search') : Text[250];
    VAR
      FieldL@1109400003 : Record 2000000041;
      RRefL@1109400010 : RecordRef;
      FRefL@1109400007 : FieldRef;
      FieldValL@1109400005 : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      IF (VehicleP.VIN = '') AND (SourceP <> SourceP::"Vehicle Search") THEN
        EXIT('');
      IF NOT FieldL.GET(DATABASE::Vehicle, FieldP) THEN
        EXIT('');
      IF NOT FieldL.Enabled THEN
        EXIT('');
      RRefL.GETTABLE(VehicleP);
      FRefL := RRefL.FIELD(FieldP);
      IF FieldL.Class = FieldL.Class::FlowField THEN
        FRefL.CALCFIELD;
      IF (FieldL.Type = FieldL.Type::Text) OR (FieldL.Type = FieldL.Type::Code) THEN
        FieldValL := FRefL.VALUE
      ELSE
        IF SourceP = SourceP::"Vehicle Search" THEN BEGIN
          IF FieldL.Type = FieldL.Type::Option THEN
            FieldValL := FORMAT(FRefL.VALUE, 0, 2)
          ELSE
            FieldValL := FORMAT(FRefL.VALUE);
        END ELSE
          FieldValL := FORMAT(FRefL.VALUE);
      EXIT(FieldValL);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ChangeVerRes@20(OldVehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400;NewVehicleP@1109400001 : Record 5025400);
    BEGIN
      // @ Function to Change the Vehicle Resouce

      // Start PA034989.21084
      IF OldVehicleP.VIN = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      OldVehicleP.CALCFIELDS("Is Resource");
      IF NOT OldVehicleP."Is Resource" THEN
        EXIT;

      ResourceG.SETRANGE(VIN, OldVehicleP.VIN);
      ResourceG.FINDFIRST;

      IF NewVehicleP.VIN = '' THEN BEGIN
        ResourceG.DELETE;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF NewVehicleP.VIN <> OldVehicleP.VIN THEN BEGIN
        ResourceG.VIN := NewVehicleP.VIN;
        ResourceG.MODIFY;
        EXIT;
      END;

      IF (NewVehicleP.Model <> OldVehicleP.Model) OR (NewVehicleP."License No." <> OldVehicleP."License No.") THEN
        ResourceG.VALIDATE("Last Name", COPYSTR(NewVehicleP.Model + ' ' + NewVehicleP.Type, 1, MAXSTRLEN(ResourceG."Last Name")));
      // Stop PA034989.21084

      IF (NewVehicleP."License No." <> OldVehicleP."License No.") THEN
        ResourceG."Search Name" := NewVehicleP."License No.";
      ResourceG.MODIFY;
    END;

    PROCEDURE InsertVehRes@18(NewVehicleP@1109400000 : Record 5025400);
    VAR
      VehiclePictureL@1109400001 : Record 5025507;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA034989
      ResourceG.Type := ResourceG.Type::Vehicle;
      ResourceG.VALIDATE("Last Name", COPYSTR(NewVehicleP.Model + ' ' + NewVehicleP.Type, 1, MAXSTRLEN(ResourceG."Last Name")));
      ResourceG."Search Name" := NewVehicleP."License No.";
      ResourceG.VIN := NewVehicleP.VIN;
      // Stop PA034989
      ResourcesSetupG.GET();
      // Start PA032862
      // Stop PA032862
      // Start PA035597
      ResourceG."Global Dimension 1 Code" := NewVehicleP."Department Code";
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA032862
      // Stop PA032862
      // Start PA035597
      ResourceG."Global Dimension 2 Code" := NewVehicleP."Make Code";
      // Stop PA035597
      // Start PA032862
      ResourceG."Main Company" := TRUE;
      // Stop PA032862
      VehiclePictureL.RESET;
      VehiclePictureL.SETRANGE(VIN, NewVehicleP.VIN);
      IF VehiclePictureL.FINDFIRST THEN
        ResourceG.Picture := VehiclePictureL.Picture;
      // Start PA034989
      // Start PA032441
      IF NOT ResourceG.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
      // Stop PA032441
        ResourceG.MODIFY(TRUE);
      // Stop PA034989
      VehicleG.GET(NewVehicleP.VIN);
    END;

    PROCEDURE FormatVehStatus@21(ForStatusP@1109400000 : Integer) : Text[30];
    VAR
      VehL@1109400001 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      VehL."Vehicle Status" := ForStatusP;
      EXIT(FORMAT(VehL."Vehicle Status"));

    PROCEDURE CalculateDaysCarriedPurReceipt@23(VINP@1109400000 : Code[20]) DaysCarriedR : Integer;
    VAR
      StartingDateL@1109400001 : Date;
      EndDateL@1109400002 : Date;
    BEGIN
      // @ Calculate days carried since the purchase receipt
      IF "Purchase Receipt Date" <> 0D THEN BEGIN
        StartingDateL := "Purchase Receipt Date";
        IF "Date of Sale" <> 0D THEN
          EndDateL := "Date of Sale"
        ELSE
          IF "Neg. Adjmt. Date" <> 0D THEN
            EndDateL := "Neg. Adjmt. Date"
          ELSE
            EndDateL := TODAY;
        DaysCarriedR := EndDateL - StartingDateL;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateDaysCarriedPurInvoice@24(VINP@1109400000 : Code[20]) DaysCarriedR : Integer;
    VAR
      StartingDateL@1109400001 : Date;
      EndDateL@1109400002 : Date;
    BEGIN
      // @ Calculate days carried since the purchase invoice
      IF "Purchase Invoice Date" <> 0D THEN BEGIN
        StartingDateL := "Purchase Invoice Date";
        IF "Date of Sale" <> 0D THEN
          EndDateL := "Date of Sale"
        ELSE
          IF "Neg. Adjmt. Date" <> 0D THEN
            EndDateL := "Neg. Adjmt. Date"
          ELSE
            EndDateL := TODAY;
        DaysCarriedR := EndDateL - StartingDateL;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckforDiffentialTaxation@1109400002(VINP@1109400000 : Code[20];BookNoP@1109400001 : Code[20];DocTypeP@1109400002 : 'Quote,Order,Invoice,Credit Memo,Blanket Order,Return Order');
    VAR
      ItemLedgEntryL@1109400006 : Record 32;
      SalesLineL@1109400005 : Record 37;
      SumInvdL@1109400003 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN, "Book No.");
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, VINP);
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.", BookNoP);
      // Start EU.0152364.151087
      ItemLedgEntryL.SETRANGE("Item No.","Model No.");
      // Stop EU.0152364.151087
      SumInvdL := 0;
      IF ItemLedgEntryL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          SumInvdL := SumInvdL + ItemLedgEntryL."Invoiced Quantity";
        UNTIL ItemLedgEntryL.NEXT = 0;
      IF SumInvdL < 0 THEN
        ERROR(C_INC047, Rec.TABLECAPTION)
      ELSE BEGIN
        SalesLineL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, VINP);
        SalesLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", DocTypeP::Order);
        IF SalesLineL.FINDFIRST THEN
          IF SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type" = SalesLineL."VAT Calculation Type"::"Differential Tax" THEN
            MESSAGE(C_INC046, Rec.TABLECAPTION, SalesLineL."Document No.", Rec.TABLECAPTION);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DateLastServOrdDrillDown@1109400008();
    VAR
      ArchServHdrL@1109400002 : Record 5025636;
      ServHdrL@1109400003 : Record 5025624;
      DateLastClosedServOrdL@1109400000 : Date;
      DateLastOpenServOrdL@1109400001 : Date;
    BEGIN
      DateLastOpenServOrdL := DateLastOpenServOrdGet(ServHdrL);
      DateLastClosedServOrdL := DateLastClosedServOrdGet(ArchServHdrL);
      IF (DateLastOpenServOrdL = 0D) AND (DateLastClosedServOrdL = 0D) THEN
        EXIT;
      IF DateLastOpenServOrdL > DateLastClosedServOrdL THEN BEGIN
        ServHdrL.MARK(TRUE);
        ServHdrL.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
        PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ServHdrL);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        ArchServHdrL.MARK(TRUE);
        ArchServHdrL.MARKEDONLY(TRUE);
        PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, ArchServHdrL);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DateLastServOrdGet@1109400004() : Date;
    VAR
      ArchServHdrL@1109400002 : Record 5025636;
      ServHdrL@1109400003 : Record 5025624;
      DateLastClosedServOrdL@1109400000 : Date;
      DateLastOpenServOrdL@1109400001 : Date;
    BEGIN
      DateLastOpenServOrdL := DateLastOpenServOrdGet(ServHdrL);
      DateLastClosedServOrdL := DateLastClosedServOrdGet(ArchServHdrL);
      IF DateLastOpenServOrdL = 0D THEN
        EXIT(DateLastClosedServOrdL);
      IF DateLastClosedServOrdL = 0D THEN
        EXIT(DateLastOpenServOrdL);
      IF DateLastOpenServOrdL > DateLastClosedServOrdL THEN
        EXIT(DateLastOpenServOrdL);
      EXIT(DateLastClosedServOrdL);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DateLastClosedServOrdGet@1109400006(VAR ArchServHdrP@1109400000 : Record 5025636) : Date;
    BEGIN
      ArchServHdrP.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN, "Order Date", "Reason for Archiving");
      ArchServHdrP.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      ArchServHdrP.SETFILTER("Reason for Archiving", '<>%1', ArchServHdrP."Reason for Archiving"::"Delete Manually without Posting");
      IF ArchServHdrP.FINDLAST THEN
        EXIT(ArchServHdrP."Order Date");
      EXIT(0D);
    END;

    PROCEDURE DateLastOpenServOrdGet@1109400005(VAR ServHdrP@1109400000 : Record 5025624) : Date;
    BEGIN
      ServHdrP.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN, "Order Date", "Branch Code");
      ServHdrP.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      IF ServHdrP.FINDLAST THEN
        EXIT(ServHdrP."Order Date");
      EXIT(0D);
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchOpenServiceOrder@1119418000(VINP@1119418000 : Code[20];VAR DocWarningP@1119418005 : TEMPORARY Record 5045369;ShowDocWarningP@1119418004 : Boolean);
    VAR
      ServHdrL@1119418002 : Record 5025624;
      ServLineL@1119418001 : Record 5025625;
      OpenServOrderExistsL@1119418003 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      ServHdrL.RESET;
      ServHdrL.SETCURRENTKEY("Document Type", VIN);
      ServHdrL.SETRANGE("Document Type", ServHdrL."Document Type"::Order);
      ServHdrL.SETRANGE(VIN, VINP);
      IF ServHdrL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          OpenServOrderExistsL := FALSE;
          ServLineL.RESET;
          ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document Type", ServLineL."Document Type"::Order);
          ServLineL.SETRANGE("Document No.", ServHdrL."No.");
          IF ServLineL.FINDSET THEN
            REPEAT
              IF ServLineL.Quantity <> ServLineL."Quantity Invoiced" THEN BEGIN
                OpenServOrderExistsL := TRUE;
                IF ShowDocWarningP THEN BEGIN
          // Start EU.0200720.202488
                  DocWarningP.AddServiceWarningLine('C_INC_ForVehicleAnOpenServiceOrderExists',
                    ServHdrL,
                    ServLineL,
                    DocWarningP."Error Type"::" ",
                    STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_ForVehicleAnOpenServiceOrderExists, ServHdrL.VIN, ServHdrL."No."),
                    DocWarningP.Category::Error);
                END ELSE
                  ERROR(C_INC_ForVehicleAnOpenServiceOrderExists, ServHdrL.VIN, ServHdrL."No.");
          // Stop EU.0200720.202488
              END;
            UNTIL (ServLineL.NEXT = 0) OR OpenServOrderExistsL;
        UNTIL ServHdrL.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE RenameImportCosting@1101353003();
    VAR
      ImportCostingLineL@1101353005 : Record 5087001;
      ImportCostingLine2L@1101353004 : Record 5087001;
      PostedImportCostingLineL@1101353003 : Record 5087006;
      PostedImportCostingLine2L@1101353002 : Record 5087006;

    BEGIN

        ImportCostingLineL.RESET;
      // Start PA033200

        ImportCostingLedgeEntry2L.RESET;
        IF MultipleCompaniesVINRenameG THEN BEGIN
          ImportCostingLineL.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
          ImportCostingLine2L.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
          PostedImportCostingLineL.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
          PostedImportCostingLine2L.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
          ImportCostingLedgeEntryL.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
          ImportCostingLedgeEntry2L.CHANGECOMPANY(RenameVINForCompanyG);
        END;
      // Stop PA033200
        ImportCostingLineL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        ImportCostingLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, xRec.VIN);
        IF ImportCostingLineL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            ImportCostingLine2L := ImportCostingLineL;
            ImportCostingLine2L.VIN := VIN;
            ImportCostingLine2L.MODIFY;
          UNTIL ImportCostingLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start PA033200
      // Stop PA033200
        PostedImportCostingLineL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        PostedImportCostingLineL.SETRANGE(VIN, xRec.VIN);
        IF PostedImportCostingLineL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            PostedImportCostingLine2L := PostedImportCostingLineL;
            PostedImportCostingLine2L.VIN := VIN;
            PostedImportCostingLine2L.MODIFY;
          UNTIL PostedImportCostingLineL.NEXT = 0;
      // Start PA033200
      // Stop PA033200
        ImportCostingLedgeEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY(VIN);
        ImportCostingLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, xRec.VIN);
        IF ImportCostingLedgeEntryL.FINDSET THEN
          REPEAT
            ImportCostingLedgeEntry2L := ImportCostingLedgeEntryL;
            ImportCostingLedgeEntry2L.VIN := VIN;
            ImportCostingLedgeEntry2L.MODIFY;
          UNTIL ImportCostingLineL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreateVehStatusChangeNewDoc@1119432000(VINP@1115000000 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      BranchOrderHdrL@1119432002 : Record 5025370;
      VehicleL@1115000001 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // @ Creates the Branch Order document and opens the corresponding card form.
      // Start PA032913
      IF VINP = '' THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_VinMustBeFilled);
      IF VehicleL.GET(VINP) AND
         NOT (VehicleL."Vehicle Status" IN [
         VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"New Vehicle",
         VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Demo Vehicle",
         VehicleL."Vehicle Status"::"Used Vehicle"])
      THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_VehStatChangeNotAllowed, VehicleL.FIELDCAPTION("Vehicle Status"), VehicleL."Vehicle Status");
      BranchOrderHdrL.INIT;
      BranchOrderHdrL."Document Type" := BranchOrderHdrL."Document Type"::"Changing Vehicle Status";
      BranchOrderHdrL.INSERT(TRUE);
      BranchOrderHdrL.VALIDATE(VIN, VINP);
      BranchOrderHdrL.MODIFY(TRUE);
      BranchOrderHdrL.SETRECFILTER;
      PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Branch Order Veh. Stat. Change", BranchOrderHdrL);
      // Stop PA032913
    END;

    PROCEDURE RenameVinOverAllCompanies@1100409000();
    VAR
      CompanyL@1100409000 : Record 2000000006;
      VehicleL@1100409001 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // Start PA033200
      IF MultipleCompaniesVINRenameG THEN BEGIN

        REPEAT
          IF CompanyL.Name <> COMPANYNAME THEN BEGIN
            VehicleL.RESET;

          END;
        UNTIL CompanyL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA033200
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchVehicleIsSold@1101277136(VINP@1119418000 : Code[20];BookNoP@1101277136 : Code[20];LineNoP@1101277138 : Integer;VAR DocWarningP@1119418005 : TEMPORARY Record 5045369;ShowDocWarningP@1119418004 : Boolean);
    VAR
      VehLedgeEntryL@1101277137 : Record 5025405;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches if Vehicle with given Book No. is sold.
      // @ param VinP - Vehicle's VIN
      // @ param BookNoP - Book No. to search for
      // @ param LineNoP - integer
      // @ param DocumentWarningP - VAR Document Warning to be created
      // @ param ShowDocWarningP - Boolean if Document Warning should be created

      // Start PA033019.9233031
      VehLedgeEntryL.RESET;
      // Start EU.0124939.125561
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry Type", VIN, "Book No.", Vehicle, Type);
      // Stop EU.0124939.125561
      // Start PA045502
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETFILTER("Entry Type", '%1|%2', VehLedgeEntryL."Entry Type"::Sale, VehLedgeEntryL."Entry Type"::Transfer);
      // Stop PA045502
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, VINP);
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.", BookNoP);
      // Start PA044453
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(Vehicle, TRUE);
      // Stop PA044453
      // Start PA039974
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(Type, VehLedgeEntryL.Type::Item);
      // Stop PA039974
      IF NOT VehLedgeEntryL.ISEMPTY THEN
      // Start PA036499
        IF VehLedgeEntryL.FINDLAST THEN
          IF NOT ItemLedgEntryIsOpen(VehLedgeEntryL) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop PA036499
            IF ShowDocWarningP THEN BEGIN
              DocWarningP.INIT;
              DocWarningP."Entry No." := DocWarningP."Entry No." + 1;
              DocWarningP."Error Type" := DocWarningP."Error Type"::Field;
              DocWarningP."Line Type" := DocWarningP."Line Type"::Vehicle;
              DocWarningP.Category := DocWarningP.Category::Error;
              DocWarningP.Area := DocWarningP.Area::"Vehicle Sales";
              DocWarningP."Document Type" := 1;
              DocWarningP."No." := VehLedgeEntryL.VIN;
              DocWarningP."Document No." := VehLedgeEntryL."Document No.";
              DocWarningP."Document Line No." := LineNoP;
              DocWarningP.Description := STRSUBSTNO(C_INC_VehicleIsSold, VINP, BookNoP, VehLedgeEntryL."Document No.");
              DocWarningP.INSERT;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              ERROR(C_INC_VehicleIsSold, VINP, BookNoP, VehLedgeEntryL."Document No.");
            END;
          END;
      // Stop PA033019.9233031
    END;

    PROCEDURE SearchVehicleIsSoldNoError@1101277137(VinP@1101277136 : Code[20];BookNoP@1101277137 : Code[20]) : Boolean;
    VAR
      VehLedgeEntryL@1101277138 : Record 5025405;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function searches if Vehicle with given Book No. is sold. withoud creating an error.
      // @ param VinP - Vehicle's VIN
      // @ param BookNoP - Book No. to search for
      // @ retval Boolean

      // Start PA033019.9299448
      VehLedgeEntryL.RESET;
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETCURRENTKEY("Entry Type", VIN, "Book No.", "Posting Date", "Department Code", Vehicle,
        "Not Relevant for Statistics", "Salespers./Purch. Code", "Make Code", "Market Segment Code", "Vehicle Category Code",
        "No.", "Vehicle Type Code");
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE("Entry Type", VehLedgeEntryL."Entry Type"::Sale);
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(VIN, VinP);
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE("Book No.", BookNoP);
      VehLedgeEntryL.SETRANGE(Vehicle, TRUE);
      IF VehLedgeEntryL.ISEMPTY THEN
        EXIT(FALSE);
      IF VehLedgeEntryL.FINDLAST THEN
        IF NOT VehLedgeEntryL."Credit Memo" THEN
          EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop PA033019.9299448
    END;

    PROCEDURE UpdateBookNoInSalesIncLines@1101286982();

    END;

    PROCEDURE HasAccessControl@1109400009() : Boolean;
    VAR
      AccessControlL@1109400000 : Record 2000000053;
      PermissionL@1109400001 : Record 2000000005;
      TenantPermissionL@16439800 : Record 2000000166;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function checks if user has access in the Company and permission to read from the Vehicle table
      // @ retval - boolean

      // Start EU.0194006.194972
      IF CURRENTCLIENTTYPE IN [CLIENTTYPE::Background, CLIENTTYPE::NAS] THEN
        EXIT(TRUE);
      // Stop EU.0194006.194972
      // Start PA041093.65483
      AccessControlL.RESET;
      AccessControlL.SETRANGE("User Security ID", USERSECURITYID);
      AccessControlL.SETFILTER("Company Name", '%1|%2', CompanyG.Name, '');
      IF AccessControlL.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          PermissionL.RESET;
          PermissionL.SETRANGE("Role ID", AccessControlL."Role ID");
          PermissionL.SETRANGE("Object Type", PermissionL."Object Type"::"Table Data");
          PermissionL.SETFILTER("Object ID", '%1|%2', 0, DATABASE::Vehicle);
          PermissionL.SETRANGE("Read Permission", PermissionL."Read Permission"::Yes);
          IF NOT PermissionL.ISEMPTY THEN
      // Start EU.0164398.165105
            EXIT(TRUE)
          ELSE BEGIN
            TenantPermissionL.RESET;
            TenantPermissionL.SETRANGE("Role ID", AccessControlL."Role ID");
            TenantPermissionL.SETRANGE("Object Type", PermissionL."Object Type"::"Table Data");
            TenantPermissionL.SETFILTER("Object ID", '%1|%2', 0, DATABASE::Vehicle);
            TenantPermissionL.SETRANGE("Read Permission", PermissionL."Read Permission"::Yes);
            IF NOT TenantPermissionL.ISEMPTY THEN
              EXIT(TRUE);
          END;
      // Stop EU.0164398.165105
        UNTIL AccessControlL.NEXT = 0;
      END;
      EXIT(FALSE);
      // Stop PA041093.65483
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE UpdateContactNoInToDos@1055600();
    VAR
      ToDoL@1055602 : Record 5080;
      ContL@1055604 : Record 5050;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function updates the contact no. for open to-dos which are
      // @ connected with vehicle appointments.
      // Start PA042646.85679
      IF NOT ContL.GET("Contact No.") THEN
        EXIT;
      ToDoL.RESET;
      ToDoL.SETRANGE(VIN, VIN);
      ToDoL.SETRANGE(Closed, FALSE);
      IF ToDoL.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ToDoL."Contact No." := "Contact No.";
          ToDoL."Contact Company No." := ContL."Company No.";
          ToDoL.MODIFY;
        UNTIL ToDoL.NEXT = 0;
      // Stop PA042646.85679
    END;

    PROCEDURE CreatePartsSalesDocument@1055601(DocumentTypeP@1119432000 : 'Quote,Order,Invoice,Credit Memo,Blanket Order,Return Order';VehicleP@1119432003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      SalesHeaderL@1119432002 : Record 36;
    BEGIN
      // @ Creates the parts sales document and opens the corresponding card Page based 'Document Type'.
      // Start PA041187.89155
      IF VehicleP = '' THEN
        ERROR(C_INC_MustNotBeBlank, FIELDCAPTION(VIN));

      SalesHeaderL.INIT;
      SalesHeaderL."Order Type" := SalesHeaderL."Order Type"::"Parts Sales & Purchases";
      SalesHeaderL."Document Type" := DocumentTypeP;
      SalesHeaderL.INSERT(TRUE);
      SalesHeaderL.VALIDATE("Supply VIN", VehicleP);
      SalesHeaderL.MODIFY(TRUE);
      SalesHeaderL.DisplayRemarksWindow();
      CASE SalesHeaderL."Document Type" OF
        SalesHeaderL."Document Type"::Order:
          PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Parts Sales Order", SalesHeaderL);
        SalesHeaderL."Document Type"::Quote:
          PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Parts Sales Quote", SalesHeaderL);
        SalesHeaderL."Document Type"::Invoice:
          PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Parts Sales Invoice", SalesHeaderL);
        SalesHeaderL."Document Type"::"Credit Memo":
          PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Parts Sales Credit Memo", SalesHeaderL);
        SalesHeaderL."Document Type"::"Return Order":
          PAGE.RUN(PAGE::"Sales Return Order", SalesHeaderL);
      END;
      // Start PA041187.89155
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckCreateUpdateLicense@4500(LicenseNoP@49701 : Code[11];ReferenceVINP@49700 : Code[17];TriggeredFromFieldP@49703 : Boolean;DisplayConfirmP@4400 : Boolean) : Code[20];
    VAR
      VehicleL@49702 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function checks the "License No." and "VIN" in combination. Aim is to refresh the License No in the Vehicle record.
      // @ When a different Vehicle with the same "License No." exists a warning message is shown.
      // @ param LicenseNoP the current license entered in vehicle documents.
      // @ param ReferenceVINP the current VIN entered in vehicle documents.
      // @ param TriggeredFromFieldP defines if the call is triggered from the entry of a "License No." field.
      // @ param DisplayConfirmP defines whether confirmation message should be displayed or not
      // @ Return Value: The VIN of the refrence Vehicle OR when the ReferenceVINP was blank the found VIN after the VehicleSearch function was triggered
      // Start EU.0000044
      IF NOT TriggeredFromFieldP THEN
        EXIT;
      // Start EU.0160054.160309
      IF (ReferenceVINP > '') AND (LicenseNoP > '') THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0160054.160309
        VehicleL.RESET;
        VehicleL.SETRANGE("License No. Compressed", CompressLicenseNo(LicenseNoP));
        VehicleL.SETFILTER(VIN, '<>%1', ReferenceVINP);
      // Start EU.0158119.158915
      // Start EU.0160054.160248
      // Start EU.0160054.160309
        VehicleL.SETFILTER("License No.", '<>%1', '');
        IF VehicleL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0160054.160309
      // Stop EU.0160054.160248
      // Stop EU.0158119.158915
          IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_DuplicateLicense, FALSE, FIELDCAPTION("License No."), LicenseNoP, TABLECAPTION, ReferenceVINP) THEN
            ERROR('');
        END ELSE BEGIN
          VehicleL.RESET;
          VehicleL.GET(ReferenceVINP);
          IF VehicleL."License No." > '' THEN
            IF DisplayConfirmP THEN
              IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_UpdateLicense, FALSE, FIELDCAPTION("License No."), TABLECAPTION, ReferenceVINP) THEN
                ERROR('');
        END;
        "License No." := LicenseNoP;
      // Start EU.0128664.129249
        "Search Description" := "License No.";
      // Stop EU.0128664.129249
        MODIFY(TRUE);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF LicenseNoP = '' THEN
          EXIT;
        ReferenceVINP := VehicleSearch(LicenseNoP);
      END;
      EXIT(ReferenceVINP);
      // Stop EU.0000044
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckVehicleLicense@49700(LicenseNoP@49701 : Code[11];ReferenceVINP@49700 : Code[17];TriggeredFromFieldP@49703 : Boolean) : Code[20];
    VAR
      VehicleL@49702 : Record 5025400;
    BEGIN
      // @ This function checks the "License No." and "VIN" in combination. Aim is to refresh the License No in the Vehicle record.
      // @ When a different Vehicle with the same "License No." exists a warning message is shown.
      // @ param LicenseNoP the current license entered in vehicle documents.
      // @ param ReferenceVINP the current VIN entered in vehicle documents.
      // @ param TriggeredFromField defines if the call is triggered from the entry of a "License No." field.
      // @ Return Value: The VIN of the refrence Vehicle OR when the ReferenceVINP was blank the found VIN after the VehicleSearch function was triggered
      // Start EU.0000497
      IF LicenseNoP = '' THEN
        EXIT;

      IF ReferenceVINP > '' THEN BEGIN
        IF VehicleL.GET(ReferenceVINP) THEN BEGIN
          VehicleL.RESET;
          VehicleL.SETRANGE("License No. Compressed", CompressLicenseNo(LicenseNoP));
          VehicleL.SETFILTER(VIN, '<>%1', ReferenceVINP);
          IF TriggeredFromFieldP THEN
      // Start EU.0177226.176218
            IF VehicleL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              IF NOT CONFIRM(C_INC_DuplicateLicense, FALSE, FIELDCAPTION("License No."), LicenseNoP, TABLECAPTION, ReferenceVINP) THEN
                ERROR('');
              VehicleL.RESET;
              VehicleL.GET(ReferenceVINP);
              VehicleL.VALIDATE("License No.", LicenseNoP);
              VehicleL.MODIFY(TRUE);
            END ELSE BEGIN
              IF CONFIRM(C_INC_UpdateLicense, FALSE, FIELDCAPTION("License No."), TABLECAPTION, ReferenceVINP) THEN BEGIN
                VehicleL.RESET;
                VehicleL.GET(ReferenceVINP);
                VehicleL.VALIDATE("License No.", LicenseNoP);
                VehicleL.MODIFY(TRUE);
              END;
            END;
      // Stop EU.0177226.176218
        END;
      END ELSE BEGIN;
        ReferenceVINP := VehicleSearch(LicenseNoP);
        IF NOT VehicleL.GET(ReferenceVINP) THEN
          ReferenceVINP := '';
      END;
      EXIT(ReferenceVINP);
      // Stop EU.0000497
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE CheckCustomerProspectData@456901(VAR OtherRecP@456903 : Record 5025400;VAR VehicleCustIsPrivateP@19176601 : Boolean);
    VAR
      OtherCustL@456900 : Record 18;
      CurrCustL@19176600 : Record 18;
      AddressesL@456901 : Record 5029111;
      CurrProspectL@456902 : Record 5050;
      OtherProspectL@19176602 : Record 5050;
    BEGIN
      // @ if not existing create Customer or Prospect from another company.
      // Start EU.0001175.6097
      // Start EU.0191766
      CurrProspectL.CHANGECOMPANY(CURRENTCOMPANY);
      CurrCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(CURRENTCOMPANY);
      OtherCustL.CHANGECOMPANY(OtherRecP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      OtherProspectL.CHANGECOMPANY(OtherRecP.CURRENTCOMPANY);
      // Start PA042760
      // Start EU.0004569
      IF OtherCustL.GET(OtherRecP."Customer No.") THEN BEGIN
        IF AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(OtherCustL."Address No.", FALSE, OtherRecP.CURRENTCOMPANY) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0004569
          IF OtherRecP."Address No." <> OtherCustL."Address No." THEN
            ERROR(C_INC030); // Error linking address no.
          CurrCustL.RESET;
          CurrCustL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
          CurrCustL.SETRANGE("Address No.", OtherCustL."Address No.");
          IF NOT CurrCustL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            AddressesL.GET(OtherCustL."Address No.");
            CurrCustL := OtherCustL;
            CurrCustL."No." := '';
      // Start PA033011
            CurrCustL."Salesperson Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Service Advisor No." := '';
            CurrCustL."Location Code" := '';
      // Stop PA033011
      // Start PA035239
            CurrCustL."Template Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Customer Posting Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Currency Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Language Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Payment Terms Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Fin. Charge Terms Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Payment Method Code" := '';
            CurrCustL."Application Method" := 0;
            CurrCustL."Gen. Bus. Posting Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Reminder Terms Code" := '';
            CurrCustL.Reserve := 0;
            CurrCustL."Labor Price Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Ext. Service Price Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Vehicle Sales Price Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Item Sales Price Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Option Sales Price Group" := '';
            CurrCustL."Add Service Surcharges" := FALSE;
      // Stop PA035239
      // Start PA043678
            CurrCustL."Credit Limit (LCY)" := 0;
            CurrCustL."Credit Limit After Sales (LCY)" := 0;
            CurrCustL."Credit Limit Vehicles (LCY)" := 0;
      // Stop PA043678
            CurrCustL.INSERT(TRUE);
      // Start PA037938.51375
            CurrCustL."Message Notification" := '';
            CurrCustL.MODIFY;
      // Stop PA037938.51375
            AddressMgntG.DEF(CURRENTCOMPANY);
            AddressMgntG.ChangeCustomer(CurrCustL, AddressesL);
          END;
          CurrProspectL.RESET;
          CurrProspectL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
          CurrProspectL.SETRANGE("Address No.", CurrCustL."Address No.");
          CurrProspectL.SETRANGE("Customer No.", CurrCustL."No.");
          CurrProspectL.SETRANGE(Type, CurrProspectL.Type::Company);
          IF NOT CurrProspectL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            CurrProspectL.SETRANGE("Customer No.", '');
            IF CurrProspectL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              CurrProspectL."Customer No." := CurrCustL."No.";
              CurrProspectL.MODIFY;
            END ELSE BEGIN
              AddressMgntG.DEF(CURRENTCOMPANY);
              AddressMgntG.MakeProspect(AddressesL);
            END;
          END;
          "Customer No." := CurrCustL."No.";
      // Start EU.0004569
        END ELSE
          VehicleCustIsPrivateP := TRUE;
      END;
      // Stop EU.0004569
      IF (OtherRecP."Vehicle Status" = OtherRecP."Vehicle Status"::"Prospect Vehicle") AND (OtherRecP."Customer No." = '') THEN BEGIN
      // Start EU.0004569
        IF OtherProspectL.GET(OtherRecP."Contact No.") THEN BEGIN
          IF AddressPrivacyMgtG.CheckAddrPrivacyValidity(OtherRecP."Address No.", FALSE, OtherRecP.CURRENTCOMPANY) THEN BEGIN
      // Stop EU.0004569
            CurrProspectL.RESET;
            CurrProspectL.SETCURRENTKEY("Address No.");
            CurrProspectL.SETRANGE("Address No.", OtherRecP."Address No.");
            CurrProspectL.SETRANGE(Type, CurrProspectL.Type::Company);
            IF NOT CurrProspectL.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              AddressesL.GET(OtherRecP."Address No.");
              AddressMgntG.DEF(CURRENTCOMPANY);
              AddressMgntG.MakeProspect(AddressesL);
            END;
      // Start EU.0004569
          END ELSE
            VehicleCustIsPrivateP := TRUE;
      // Stop EU.0191766
        END;
      // Stop EU.0004569
      END;
      // Stop PA042760
      // Stop EU.0001175.6097
    END;

    BEGIN
